Meridian — development log
==========================

A chronological, append-only stream of decisions, hand-offs, and "why we
did it this way" notes. Every agent (human or sub-agent) that does real
work on the repo appends a short entry. One log, many voices. Newest at
the bottom.

Format for each entry:
  [YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM TZ] <role@agent-name> — <one-line summary>
  <1-6 lines of context / decision / hand-off>

----------------------------------------------------------------------

[2026-04-24 20:40 UTC] principal@meridian-labs — repo scaffolding + ADRs 0001, 0002
Branched claude/ai-agent-orchestrator-hAmzy. Laid down CLAUDE.md with the
non-negotiables (LLM-agnostic, local-first, privacy tiers, agents-as-data,
replay). Wrote ADR 0001 (agent.v1 spec + engine interfaces) and ADR 0002
(tech stack: TypeScript on Bun, Postgres+pgvector, OTEL→Langfuse, native
provider SDKs, not LiteLLM). Wrote docs/deploy/free-tier-dev.md so the
whole stack boots on free tiers (Vercel + Fly.io + Neon + R2 + Upstash
+ E2B + Gemini/Groq/Ollama).

[2026-04-24 21:18 UTC] principal — starting wave 2 (engineering)
Scaffolded monorepo root (package.json, pnpm-workspace.yaml,

[2026-04-24 21:22 UTC] backend@registry-engineer — platform/registry v0
Shipped @meridian/registry: Zod schema for agent.v1 (strict, snake_case
on disk), YAML loader with snake->camel transform, public validate(),
in-memory storage with semver + promoted-version pointer, AgentRegistry
impl of the @meridian/types interface, thin `semver` helpers. Fixtures
cover the ADR 0001 code-reviewer example plus a missing-model_policy
negative case. 19 vitest tests pass; tsc strict + biome clean. Two
notable calls that affect other packages: (1) escalation accepts either
a bare array OR the ADR-0001 `{on: [...]}` wrapper and normalises to
an array in AgentSpec; (2) AgentRegistry.load(ref) without a version
returns the promoted pointer, falls back to the single-version case as
a bootstrap convenience, otherwise throws NoPromotedVersionError.
Postgres storage and typed EvalReport gating are marked TODO(v1).

[2026-04-24 21:13 UTC] backend — platform/observability v0
Delivered OTEL-backed Tracer, GenAI/Meridian attribute helpers, an
in-memory replay store with versioned encode/decode, and a Postgres
exporter stub. 11 files, 21 vitest tests pass; tsc strict + biome clean.
Adopted OTEL GenAI semantic conventions (gen_ai.system, gen_ai.request.*,
gen_ai.response.*, gen_ai.usage.input_tokens / output_tokens, gen_ai.tool.*,
gen_ai.operation.name = chat | execute_tool). All Meridian span kinds
map to OTEL INTERNAL; the kind is also carried on meridian.span.kind.
Replay payload lives under meridian.* (run, trace, node, agent, policy,
memory, cost, budget, rng). No provider names in keys — provider is a
value of gen_ai.system. Gap for next engineer: PostgresSpanExporter is
a shape-only stub — needs a real writer (Neon serverless preferred)
plus an OTEL SpanProcessor bridge so finished spans flow into the
table defined in exporter-postgres.ts. Langfuse exporter deferred.

[2026-04-24 21:15 UTC] backend@cli-engineer — apps/cli v0 scaffold
Shipped @meridian/cli (the `meridian` binary) with commander-driven argv
parsing and an injectable CliIO so tests can drive `main(argv)` and
capture stdout/stderr. Real commands: `init`, `agent new`, `agent
validate`, `agent ls`. Stubs that exit 2 and point to
docs/deploy/free-tier-dev.md: `run`, `runs ls`, `runs view`, `models ls`,
`mcp ls`, `dev`. `--json` is wired on validate / ls / init / run / dev.
SIGINT prints `(interrupted)` and exits 130. 23 files, 16 vitest tests
pass; tsc strict + biome clean. `bun build --compile` script wired but
not run. Registry integration goes through `src/registry-adapter.ts`:
the registry has no root `index.ts` yet, so the adapter dynamic-imports
`@meridian/registry/src/validator.js` via a runtime-assembled specifier
and falls back to a bootable stub. Tests inject a fake RegistryLike via
`setRegistry`. Assumed public surface: `validate(yaml: string):
ValidationResult` — matches @meridian/types. When the registry ships a
root export, swap the specifier; no call sites change.

[2026-04-24 21:17 UTC] backend@engine-engineer — platform/engine v0
Shipped @meridian/engine: Runtime with spawn-permission enforcement and
parent/child tracking, LeafAgentRun implementing the per-turn loop
(messages → ModelGateway.complete → tool dispatch via ToolHost → loop
until finishReason==='stop'), AbortController wired through ctx.signal
so cancel() propagates to gateway calls, InMemoryCheckpointer capturing
messages + tool-results + rngSeed + overrides at every pre/post node
boundary, and a full Orchestrator that walks Graph trees. Node runners:
pipeline, supervisor, parallel (all|first|quorum with loser-cancel on
'first'), router (label or JSON.branch), debate (N rounds + judge),
subscription (EventBus-backed, lives until graph cancel), agent leaf.
Stores: InMemoryMemoryStore (scope-aware), InProcessEventBus (pattern
wildcards), permissive RuleChainPolicyEngine, NoopTracer. 27 files;
8 vitest tests pass covering spawn tree, spawn-permission rejection,
cancel-aborts-in-flight, pipeline order, parallel(first) returns
immediately, supervisor parallel fan-out, checkpoint+resume-with-model-
override. tsc strict + biome clean. Contract assumptions from other
packages: (1) ModelGateway implementations read ctx.signal — the type
in @meridian/types doesn't declare a signal field, but cancellation
requires it; engine passes an augmented context. Worth formalising as
a non-breaking `readonly signal?: AbortSignal` on CallContext. (2) The
registry returns a fully-hydrated AgentSpec — engine does not read
systemFile from disk (synthesises a minimal prompt from identity only);
TODO(v1) once the registry exposes a resolved-prompt field. (3) The
ModelDescriptor's id+provider is round-trip-stable enough that a
resume-with-override can re-request the same model deterministically.

[2026-04-24 21:40 UTC] tech-writer — reference agency committed
Wrote the initial 26-agent reference set under agency/: 4 direction, 7
delivery, 11 support, 4 meta, each with a meridian/agent.v1 YAML and a
companion prompts/<name>.system.md. All specs parse, all required top-
level keys present, every prompt file referenced exists on disk. Kept
the specs LLM-agnostic via capability_class (reasoning-large / medium /
small / local-reasoning / fast-draft); every sensitive-tier agent carries
a local-reasoning fallback so on-prem tenants can stay on-prem. Eval
gates and budgets drafted per role — numbers are first-pass and will
tighten once the harness lands. Reporting lines form a single tree with
principal at the root; only supervisors (principal, architect, tech-lead,
hr) spawn; reviewers and auditors never spawn.

[2026-04-24 21:18 UTC] backend@gateway-engineer — platform/gateway v0
Shipped @meridian/gateway: capability-class router + adapter registry +
provider-agnostic ModelGateway. 21 files, 20 vitest tests (router,
pricing, registry, end-to-end via mock adapter); tsc strict + biome
clean. Real adapter code for openai-compat (covers OpenAI/Ollama/vLLM/
llama.cpp/LM Studio/Groq/OpenRouter/TGI), native Anthropic (tool_use
SSE), native Gemini (functionCall SSE); xai piggy-backs on openai-compat;
bedrock is a typed stub. Chose hand-rolled fetch over provider SDKs —
ADR 0002 agrees. Constrained-decoding helpers emit response_format +
guided_json/guided_grammar; JSON-Schema→GBNF compiler is a TODO(v1).
One cross-package design call worth flagging: RegisteredModel extends
ModelDescriptor with a `providerKind` tag that lives in this package
only, not in @meridian/types. Router dispatch uses this string to look
up adapters, keeping the types package free of any provider enum.
Callers passing hydrated ModelDescriptors from other packages will need
to carry providerKind + providerConfig alongside (or rely on the gateway's
own registry for dispatch).

[2026-04-24 UTC] engine-researcher — wrote docs/research/engine-landscape.md
Compared LangGraph, CrewAI, AutoGen v0.4, OpenAI Agents SDK, Semantic
Kernel, smolagents, Temporal/Restate, Inngest/Trigger.dev, Pydantic-AI,
Mastra. Pattern matrix shows no framework natively covers all six
patterns and none enforce privacy tiers. Confirmed ADR 0002: build
custom engine on TS+Bun+Postgres-checkpointer; Mastra closest fit but
still leaves gateway/privacy/eval to us. Defer Temporal adapter to ADR
0003. Build: graph exec, checkpointer, HITL store. Buy: scheduler
(graphile-worker/pg-boss), OTEL, Langfuse v0. Status: proposed.

[2026-04-24 22:24 UTC] backend-engineer — Postgres persistence: registry + engine
Wired durable storage end-to-end. New @meridian/storage package owns
SqlClient (driver-agnostic wrapper over node-postgres / Neon serverless
/ pglite), a forward-only migration runner, the canonical 001_init.sql
(tenants, agents, agent_versions, runs, checkpoints, run_events,
usage_records, span_events with run_id/promoted/parent indexes), and
the Drizzle ORM schema mirroring it. Picked Drizzle over Kysely for
Neon parity (justification in the package README). Registry gained
PostgresStorage behind a new async RegistryStorage interface; the
existing InMemoryStorage stays as the test default and now exposes both
sync (legacy) and async surfaces. Engine gained PostgresCheckpointer
beside InMemoryCheckpointer; runs replay across restarts via
checkpoints.payload_jsonb. Tests (added 8): migrate idempotency on
pglite, registry round-trip / promotion / unknown-rejection, checkpoint
write-and-read fidelity. Verify: pnpm install clean, pnpm -r typecheck
clean, pnpm -r test green for storage (2), registry (23 incl. 4 new),
engine (11 incl. 3 new); other packages unchanged. DATABASE_URL is the
single config knob — fromDatabaseUrl() picks pglite/Neon/pg from the
URL, so no other package branches on driver type.

[2026-04-24 22:35 UTC] backend-engineer@meridian-labs — wave 3C: meridian-fs MCP server
Built mcp-servers/meridian-fs/ (@meridian/mcp-fs): first-party stdio MCP
server backed by @modelcontextprotocol/sdk 1.29, zod 3.25, vitest 2.1.
Five tools: fs.read / fs.write / fs.list / fs.stat / fs.search; fs.delete
and fs.move flagged TODO(v1). ACL is the security core — three layers:
lexical containment after path.resolve, per-component lstat/realpath check
to refuse symlinks pointing outside roots, final realpath check on the
target (or its deepest existing ancestor for new-file writes). Roots
declared via --roots / MERIDIAN_FS_ROOTS / --config json; spec syntax
deviated to comma-separated <abs-path>:<ro|rw> pairs (brief said colon-
separated but that breaks Windows drive letters; documented). 32 tests
across 3 files all green: traversal blocked, symlink escapes blocked,
ro-root writes refused, in-process MCP client round-trips fs.read /
fs.write via InMemoryTransport. Errors are structured {code, message}
with codes NOT_FOUND | PERMISSION_DENIED | OUT_OF_BOUNDS | TOO_LARGE |
INTERNAL. Caps: read 4MiB, write 8MiB, search 200 hits / 5000 lines /
1000 files. Least-confident security check flagged in README for the
auditor: TOCTOU between ACL realpath and the actual read/write syscall.
Mitigation candidate: openat with O_NOFOLLOW per component plus fstat
inode re-check. Touched only mcp-servers/meridian-fs/.

[2026-04-24 22:27 UTC] backend-engineer@meridian-labs — meridian run, end-to-end
Wired apps/cli/src/commands/run.ts from stub to real: loads .env via the
new platform/runtime-config glue package, builds typed Config (provider
discovery for groq/ollama/anthropic/gemini, runUsdCap, defaultPrivacy),
and bootstraps a PlatformRuntime + GatewayEx (createOpenAICompatAdapter
covers both Groq and Ollama; Anthropic/Google adapters opportunistically
registered when keyed). Per-model enablement is config-driven so a
keyless cloud descriptor never leaks into routing. Streams RunEvents to
stdout (text deltas direct, "→ tool: <name>" / "← result" prefixes);
--json buffers and dumps {ok,output,usage,model,elapsedMs}; --dry-run
calls the router only, never the adapter. MERIDIAN_RUN_USD_CAP rewrites
the spec budget before spawn. Provider-not-enabled raises a typed error
pointing at .env.example. Added Groq llama-3.3-70b-versatile / 8b-instant
and ollama.qwen2.5:7b plus ollama.qwen2.5-coder:32b descriptors to
platform/gateway/fixtures/models.yaml (kept the legacy qwen2.5-coder:32b
id so platform/gateway/tests/registry.test.ts stays green). 35 CLI tests
pass; gateway, engine, registry, observability, runtime-config all
typecheck clean. Touched: apps/cli/, platform/gateway/fixtures/models.yaml,
new platform/runtime-config/.

are configured server-side — so the UI can grey out unconfigured

[2026-04-25 06:30 UTC] backend-engineer@aldo-tech-labs — wave 4 apps/api: Hono control-plane scaffolded
Built apps/api on top of @aldo-ai/api-contract Zod schemas + @aldo-ai/storage
SqlClient. Six routes: GET /health, GET /v1/runs (cursor paged), GET
/v1/runs/:id, GET /v1/agents (cursor paged + team/owner filter), GET
/v1/agents/:name (versions[] + opaque spec), GET /v1/models (reads
platform/gateway/fixtures/models.yaml; stamps `available` from env vars
through a single provider->env mapping — no provider SDKs, no provider
constants on hot paths). Cursors are opaque base64url JSON of (at, id);
totalUsd / lastProvider / lastModel computed in SQL via a LEFT JOIN +
correlated subquery so list pages stay O(page-size). Central error
handler emits the typed ApiError envelope and turns ZodError into 400
validation_error with issues in details. CORS allows http://localhost:3000
plus CORS_ORIGINS extras. Tests (16) drive the Hono app via app.request()
backed by pglite — no port, no real network. createDeps() is the single
spot env is read; tests inject db + registry. pnpm typecheck + tests
green; biome clean for apps/api. Boots via `pnpm --filter @aldo-ai/api dev`
on PORT 3001 (HOST 0.0.0.0) after applying @aldo-ai/storage migrations.
Touched only apps/api/.

[2026-04-24 23:25 UTC] principal — smoke test passed + deploy artifacts
Booted apps/api on :3001 + apps/web on :3000 locally and curled every
route. Caught one integration bug that unit tests didn't see: Next.js
webpack couldn't resolve `.js`-suffixed imports against TypeScript
sources in workspace packages (api-contract uses Node-ESM-style
`.js` suffixes that don't match a real file). Fixed in
apps/web/next.config.mjs by adding webpack.resolve.extensionAlias
mapping `.js` -> `.ts/.tsx/.js` plus transpilePackages for
@aldo-ai/api-contract and @aldo-ai/types. After the fix every route
returns 200, /v1/models is populated from fixtures, empty-state
pagination works, /runs/[bogus] degrades gracefully, CORS preflight
returns 204 with the right allow-origin, bad cursor returns 400 with
the ApiError envelope.

Deploy artifacts shipped (option D from the wave 4 menu):
- apps/api/Dockerfile: multi-stage Node 22 alpine image with tini PID 1,
  non-root user, /health-based HEALTHCHECK, expects PORT/HOST env.
- apps/api/.dockerignore: excludes node_modules, dist, .next, docs,
  agency, mcp-servers, and the rest of the monorepo noise.
- apps/api/fly.toml: aldo-ai-api app, primary_region=iad, shared-cpu-1x
  256MB, auto_stop on idle, /health check every 30s, internal port 8080,
  CORS_ORIGINS preset.
- apps/web/vercel.json: Next.js framework preset, build command runs
  the workspace install + filtered build.
- .github/workflows/deploy-api.yml: triggers `flyctl deploy` on push to
  main when DEPLOY_API_ENABLED repo variable is `true` and FLY_API_TOKEN
  secret is set. Concurrency-grouped, 15-min timeout, paths-filtered.
- docs/deploy/getting-started.md: 30-min click-by-click walkthrough —
  Neon project, fly launch + secrets, Vercel project + env, CORS update,
  end-to-end verify.
- docs/deploy/smoke-test.md: 60-second local verify recipe + the bug we
  caught the first time.

[2026-04-25 08:08 UTC] principal — v0.2 LIVE end-to-end
Recovered through four real bugs surfaced only by production execution:
1. Build context: deploy-api.yml ran flyctl from apps/api/ — Dockerfile
   couldn't COPY ../../platform/*. Fix: run from repo root with explicit
   --config / --dockerfile flags.
2. Runtime TypeScript: workspace packages declare main: ./src/index.ts;
   Node can't load TS. Fix: tsx as runtime dep, drop the build stage,
   start with `node_modules/.bin/tsx src/index.ts`.

   sql(text,params,opts) was removed. Fix: rewrite both call sites in
   platform/storage/src/pool.ts.

   models.yaml; image only COPYed declared workspace deps. Fix: COPY
   platform/gateway too.

[2026-04-25 10:36 UTC] backend-engineer (engineer A) — wave 5 engine debugger primitives + run persistence shipped
Engine now exports BreakpointStore (InMemory + Postgres), PauseController,
editAndResume, RunStore (InMemory + Postgres), all wired into
LeafAgentRun and PlatformRuntime as opt-in deps. Per-turn loop checks
breakpoints before model_call (agent name surface) and before each
tool_call (tool name surface), persists a paused checkpoint, emits a
checkpoint event tagged paused:true, and awaits the controller; step
mode is a one-shot re-pause flag. AgentRun.editAndResume rewrites a
checkpoint message and resumes from a fresh checkpoint id (originals
preserved for audit). PauseController surfaces to the API via
subscribePause/subscribeResume callbacks; the API also sees a
checkpoint event with paused:true so it can map cleanly to the
DebugRunEvent kind:'paused' wire type without touching @aldo-ai/types.
Added migration 002_breakpoints.sql for the breakpoints table. Engine
test count: 17 (was 11), all green; storage tests still pass; biome +
typecheck clean across all 12 workspace projects. BreakpointStore
default is in-memory (Postgres is opt-in via Runtime deps). Assumed
apps/api will construct PauseController + InMemory or Postgres stores
once per process and inject them into PlatformRuntime alongside the
shared SqlClient.

in @aldo-ai/storage tracked single-quote and double-quote state but
ignored SQL `--` line and `/* */` block comments. The new
002_breakpoints migration's preamble contained "engine's" — the
apostrophe flipped inSingle=true while the splitter was inside a
comment line; the literal `'{}'::jsonb` later in the file flipped it
back off; statement boundaries got scrambled; the Neon HTTP driver
saw a fragment beginning with "for" and rejected with `42601 syntax
error`. Fixed by teaching splitSqlScript to skip line + block
comments, and by removing the apostrophe from the comment as a
belt-and-braces. Pushed in aea8605, deploy succeeded immediately.

  `secret://<name>` references at tool-call time only.

[2026-04-25 14:05 UTC] backend@wave7-engineer-B — @aldo-ai/guards landed
New workspace package with three layers: spotlighting (Simon-style
<untrusted-content source="..."> wrappers + a system-prompt prefix that
tells the model to treat inner text as data), regex output-scanner
(allowlisted URLs / base64 blobs / 13 curated prompt-leak markers
sourced from Simon Willison's writeups, OWASP LLM-Top-10 2025, MS PyRIT,
public DAN/GPTfuzzer corpora), and DualLlmQuarantine that summarises
oversized tool output through a separate ModelGateway call routed by
capability class — the privileged path never sees raw tool bytes.
Wired via a new GatewayMiddleware seam on createGateway: `before`
rewrites tool_result parts on the inbound CompletionRequest, `after`

[2026-04-25 14:11 UTC] orchestrator — wave 7 LIVE in production (recovery #7)
First deploy of wave 7 (run 24932592192) succeeded as far as Fly was
concerned but the new image crashlooped: @aldo-ai/secrets refuses to
boot in production without ALDO_SECRETS_MASTER_KEY (Engineer C's
intentional guard). Recovery: generated 32-byte base64 master key,
added it as GitHub repo secret ALDO_SECRETS_MASTER_KEY via libsodium
sealed-box (PAT-driven), and added a `flyctl secrets set --stage` step
to .github/workflows/deploy-api.yml so the secret rolls out atomically
with the image. Re-dispatched (run 24932714878) — completed success.
Smoke verified: GET /health 200; GET /v1/secrets 200 {secrets:[]}; POST
/v1/secrets returns a SecretSummary with fingerprint + preview (raw
value never echoed); GET shows the row; final GET after DELETE shows
the row gone.

Follow-up bug: DELETE /v1/secrets/:name returned 404 even when the row
existed and was successfully removed. The side-effect is correct (the
secret IS deleted) but the response code is wrong; route handler
appears to read-then-delete in the wrong order. Not a blocker —
logging for next wave.

Wave 7 lesson: when an engineer adds a "production refuses to boot
without ENV_VAR" guard, the deploy pipeline must learn the env var at
the same time the package lands. The Dockerfile-COPY-list lesson
generalizes: every wave that touches operational surface (deps, env,
migrations) must update apps/api/Dockerfile + .github/workflows/
deploy-api.yml in the same commit as the package itself.

[2026-04-25 15:16 UTC] orchestrator — wave 7 follow-up: rowCount fix (recovery #8)
Smoke DELETE bug from the wave-7 LIVE entry: traced to the Neon
adapter (platform/storage/src/pool.ts) calling sql.query with
`fullResults: false`, which makes @neondatabase/serverless return
only the rows array. For DELETE/UPDATE without RETURNING the array
is empty, and the adapter's `rowCount: rows.length` was always 0.
PostgresSecretStore.delete saw "no row affected" and the API surfaced
404 on every successful DELETE.

Switched the Neon path to `fullResults: true` and read the real
`rowCount` from the pg-style envelope. Kept `rows.length` as a fallback
in case a future Neon version omits the field on certain commands.
This also unblocks any future caller that branches on `rowCount` for
mutation queries (audit-replay logic in the registry, eval promotion
gates, etc.).

While in there: fixed the `recentAudit` flake (pglite `now()` is
ms-granular and back-to-back recordAudit calls collided on
`ORDER BY at DESC` with no tiebreak). Pass `at` explicitly with 1s
spacing in the test — production query unchanged. Suite ran clean 3x
in a row before commit.

Deployed via run 24933945400. Re-smoked: POST 200, DELETE 204, second
DELETE 404, final GET empty list. Recovery #8 closed.

[2026-04-25 16:45 UTC] Engineer G — wave 8 local discovery
Built `@aldo-ai/local-discovery` — a new platform workspace package
that probes well-known local-LLM ports (Ollama 11434/api/tags, vLLM
8000/v1/models, llama.cpp 8080/v1/models, LM Studio 1234/v1/models)
in parallel with a 1 s per-probe AbortController timeout, returning
a union of `DiscoveredModel`s that extend `RegisteredModel` with
`source` + `discoveredAt` metadata. Probes use native fetch only
(no new external deps), tolerate every failure mode (connection
refused, 404, non-JSON, wrong shape, timeout) — they NEVER throw,
just log to an injected `onDebug` and return []. Configurable via
`ALDO_LOCAL_DISCOVERY=ollama,vllm,llamacpp,lmstudio` (default all)
or `=none` to disable. Discovered models default to
`capabilityClass: 'local-reasoning'`, `locality: 'local'`,
`privacyAllowed: ['public', 'internal', 'sensitive']`,
`providerKind: 'openai-compat'`, zero-cost, baseUrl set to
`${probedBase}/v1` so the existing OpenAI-compat adapter dials
them without code changes. Files added: platform/local-discovery/
{package.json, tsconfig.json, vitest.config.ts, src/{index.ts,
discover.ts, registry-merge.ts, types.ts, probes/{util.ts,
ollama.ts, vllm.ts, llamacpp.ts, lmstudio.ts}}, tests/{util,
probes-ollama, probes-openai-compat, discover, registry-merge}
.test.ts}. Test count: 58 (5 files: util×7, ollama×8, parameter-
ised vllm/llamacpp/lmstudio×24, discover×11, merge×8) all green
in 876 ms. Wired into apps/api/src/routes/models.ts via a 30 s
process-scoped cache (singleflight via inFlight promise) — YAML
entries always win on duplicate id; discovered rows fill gaps and
are reported `available: true` since they were just observed.
Added `resetDiscoveryCache()` export so `apps/api/tests/_setup.ts`
can flush between harness instances; harness now defaults to
`ALDO_LOCAL_DISCOVERY=none` so the test suite doesn't burn its
budget on closed localhost ports — full apps/api suite drops
from 24 s back to 12 s. New `aldo models discover` subcommand
(apps/cli/src/commands/models-discover.ts) prints id|source|
capabilityClass|locality|baseUrl as a fixed-column table, exits
1 with the polite "no local LLM servers found on default ports
— start Ollama / vLLM / llama.cpp / LM Studio" message when
nothing responds, exits 0 when ≥1 model found; --json + --timeout
flags supported. Manually smoke-tested the binary path with
`tsx src/index.ts models discover`: prints the polite message
+ exits 1 on a clean dev box. Dockerfile updated (deps stage
COPY platform/local-discovery/package.json + sources stage COPY
platform/local-discovery ./platform/local-discovery) so the
deployed API ships the new dep. apps/api/package.json gained
`@aldo-ai/local-discovery` (and biome auto-hoisted the existing
transitive `@aldo-ai/gateway` to a direct dep — local-discovery
re-exports `RegisteredModel`). apps/cli/package.json + cli.ts
register the new command alongside the existing `models ls` stub.
Quality bar: pnpm -r typecheck green; pnpm exec biome check on
all new/changed files clean (8 pre-existing biome errors in other
waves' files left untouched per scope). Total tests across the
14 backend packages now 499 (was 441) — +58 from this package,
+1 in apps/api models.test (discovery-disabled sanity check),
plus the existing `agents` route gained 4 tests from a parallel
wave. LLM-agnostic verified end-to-end: nothing under
platform/gateway or apps/api keys routing on the runtime labels
ollama/vllm/llamacpp/lmstudio — they're display-only; the only
place those strings map to behaviour is the orchestrator's
internal probe registry. Privacy default `[public, internal,
sensitive]` is documented in registry-merge.ts (local inference
is the answer to the sensitive-tier non-negotiable). Decisions
worth flagging: (a) discovery cache is module-scoped not
per-Deps, since it's a process concern + saves bookkeeping —
tests reset via the exported helper; (b) effectiveContextTokens
defaults to 8192 for discovered rows (a conservative floor —
operators who want a 128k window can hand-add a YAML entry which
takes precedence); (c) the brief mentioned `providerConfig.apiKey:
''` but `RegisteredModel.providerConfig` doesn't carry an apiKey
field — confirmed in gateway/src/model-registry.ts schema —
so we set only `baseUrl`; the openai-compat adapter already
skips the Authorization header when `config.apiKey` is empty
(verified at platform/gateway/src/providers/openai-compat.ts:237).
Not committed — orchestrator integrates.

fail-closed-first and left the engine spawn for a later wave.
(3) The audit-event emission is post-success only — if the
adapter throws during streaming, no audit row fires. That
matches the wave-8 brief ("when ... actually routes
successfully") but worth confirming with the security review;
an alternative would emit on first delta. Not committed —
orchestrator integrates.

[2026-04-25 17:55 UTC] Engineer J — wave 9 orchestrator runtime
Shipped @aldo-ai/orchestrator: a multi-agent supervisor runtime
the engine delegates to whenever an AgentSpec carries a `composite:`
block. New package at platform/orchestrator with src/{types,
supervisor, cost-rollup, jsonpath, limits, privacy, index}.ts plus
src/strategies/{common,sequential,parallel,debate,iterative}.ts —
strategy-per-file, common.ts owns spawn-and-await + the
CompositeChildFailedError envelope. Public surface: `Supervisor`
class with `runComposite(spec, input, ctx)` returning an
`OrchestrationResult` ({ ok, output, children, strategy,
totalUsage, rounds? }). The engine integrates via two structural
hooks in PlatformRuntime: (a) `RuntimeDeps.orchestrator?:
CompositeOrchestrator` (or `setOrchestrator()` for the late-bind
chicken-and-egg), and (b) a new `runtime.runAgent(ref, inputs,
{parent, root})` entry point that resolves the spec and either
constructs a `LeafAgentRun` (existing path, unchanged) or wraps
the Promise<OrchestrationResult> in a tiny `CompositeAgentRun` that
satisfies the public `AgentRun` surface. Engine ↔ orchestrator
cycle avoided via a structural `CompositeOrchestrator` interface —
the engine never imports @aldo-ai/orchestrator. The orchestrator
calls back into the engine through `runtime.asSupervisorAdapter()`
which returns a `SupervisorRuntimeAdapter` (`spawnChild` +
`loadSpec`). Storage migration 005_composite_runs.sql adds
root_run_id + composite_strategy to the runs table (parent_run_id
already existed in 001), plus indices `idx_runs_root` and
`idx_runs_composite_root`; pre-existing rows are backfilled to
`root_run_id = id` so the index is dense. PostgresRunStore +
InMemoryRunStore both gained the new columns through a widened
`RunStartArgs` type; InMemoryRunStore exposes `getRun()` +
`listByRoot()` for tests + the orchestrator's tree queries.
LeafAgentRun gained `collectUsage()` — a side-channel that
captures every UsageRecord the run emits, so the orchestrator's
cost roll-up can read child usage without competing with the
single-consumer `events()` async iterable (this fix unblocked
the wave-8 usage-event tests). Five new RunEvent types added to
@aldo-ai/types and to the api-contract Zod enum (additive, no
breaking changes): composite.{child_started, child_completed,
child_failed, usage_rollup, iteration}. CompositeSpec shape
settled on (matches the type Engineer K already published in
@aldo-ai/types): `{ strategy: 'sequential'|'parallel'|'debate'
|'iterative', subagents: { agent: string, as?: string, inputMap?:
Record<string,string> }[], aggregator?: string (debate),
iteration?: { maxRounds: number, terminate: string } (iterative)
}`. The Supervisor adds a runtime-resolved `SubagentInvocation`
shape that carries the post-cascade `privacy: PrivacyTier` so
strategy code never has to peek at AgentSpec.modelPolicy directly.
Cost roll-up determinism: `sumUsage()` rounds usd to 6 decimals
(matches NUMERIC(14,6)), takes max(at) lexicographically, and
collapses divergent provider/model fields to the literal
`aldo:composite` / `multi` so two replays produce byte-equal
totalUsage records. Tests by category (45 total in
platform/orchestrator/tests/): strategy 17 (sequential 5,
parallel 4, debate 3, iterative 5), cost-rollup 8, linkage 5,
errors 9 (5 error-propagation + 4 jsonpath terminate eval),
depth-limit 3, engine-integration 3 (full PlatformRuntime ↔
Supervisor end-to-end through InMemoryRunStore including
parent/root linkage on every child + the
CompositeRuntimeMissingError fail-closed path). Quality bar:
pnpm -r typecheck green across all 14 backend packages; pnpm
lint clean (biome --write applied on 5 files for sort-imports +
delete→assignment-undefined; no remaining errors); pnpm -r test
green — orchestrator 45 (new), engine 29 (no regressions),
storage 2 (extended one to round-trip the new columns through
pglite), api-contract 18, registry 48, api 73, cli 64, all other
packages unchanged. Apps/api/Dockerfile + apps/api/package.json
updated to ship @aldo-ai/{engine, observability, orchestrator}
sources + deps (wave-6.5/7 lesson). Decisions to flag for review:
(1) The brief asked for OTEL Span Links between parent and child
runs and `composite.strategy=<name>` span attributes — the engine
does NOT currently wrap a full agent run in an OTEL span (only
sub-operations like model_call / tool_call get span() wrappers).
The composite strategy + parent_run_id are already on every
RunEvent payload and persisted on the runs row, so the linkage
exists in the run-event log; adding run-level span wrappers is
a strictly additive change that I left for a follow-up because
introducing it for composite runs only would create asymmetry
with leaf runs (which would then be the only runs without span
wrappers). Suggestion: wave-10 should add `runtime.runAgent` →
`tracer.span('agent_run', 'agent', {...})` for BOTH leaf and
composite paths uniformly. (2) The composite supervisor itself
spawns NO LeafAgentRun for the supervisor agent's prompt — the
supervisor is a pure coordinator; its self-usage in the roll-up
is the canonical zero record. If K's eval gates expect the
supervisor agent to ALSO have its own model call (a
"plan-then-delegate" pattern), wave-10 should add a pre-fan-out
Plan call. The current wiring is intentional — it minimises
tokens and keeps the cost roll-up purely about subagent work.
(3) `runtime.spawn(parent=<composite>, fromComposite=true)`
skips the `parentSpec.spawn.allowed.includes(ref.name)` check
because the supervisor's `composite.subagents[]` list is the
source of authority for that fan-out. Existing
spawn.allowed-gated explicit child spawns are unchanged. (4)
The engine's CompositeAgentRun returns a closed (immediately-
done) events() iterator — composite runs surface their children's
events through the child Run objects (which are first-class).
The api layer / debugger should walk children via parent_run_id
to render a tree. Engineer L's frontend tree visualization will
consume the existing /v1/runs/:id/tree endpoint that K wired in
wave-9 (it already returns nested run summaries by parent_run_id).
Not committed — orchestrator integrates.

Authorization-header injection strategy: hybrid server-component-first
+ proxy route. Server callers go through `lib/api.ts`'s request<T>(),

side-effect-imports + wires getSession() → setServerTokenResolver()).
Client components hit /api/auth-proxy/[...path] (route handler) which

Bearer auth — the bearer never reaches the browser bundle. Why two
paths: `lib/api.ts` is imported from existing client islands

except /login, /signup, /api/health, _next/, favicon.ico, and
/api/auth-proxy (proxy does its own session check). Middleware also
stamps `x-aldo-pathname` so the root layout can suppress the sidebar
chrome on /login + /signup without having to relocate every protected
page into a route group. Sidebar (components/sidebar.tsx) gained a
user-menu footer: avatar (initials), email, current tenant slug, and a
dropdown that lists other memberships (sidebar-actions.ts:
switchTenantAction calls /v1/auth/switch-tenant, setSession with the
new token, and revalidatePath('/', 'layout') to refresh every server
component). Logout is a server action that best-efforts /v1/auth/logout,
clearSession()s, and redirects to /login. Tests: vitest config added
(matches apps/api shape); 40 unit tests across 4 files
(lib/session.test.ts ×8 cookie shape + round-trip, lib/api.test.ts ×8
Authorization-header injection + 401 handling, lib/middleware-shared.
test.ts ×10 isPublicPath / redirectToLogin, app/(auth)/schemas.test.ts
×14 form schemas + safeNextPath whitelist). E2E: apps/web-e2e/tests/

(unconditional), and a writes-gated signup→logout→login flow with a
unique-per-run timestamped email + password (skipped unless
E2E_ALLOW_WRITES=true). Quality bar green: pnpm --filter @aldo-ai/web
typecheck clean, pnpm exec biome check apps/web platform/api-contract
clean, next build succeeds (all 20 routes compile, middleware bundle
32.4 kB), 40/40 tests pass; 18/18 api-contract tests still green
after the additive schema. Decisions to flag: (1) The brief permitted

[2026-04-25 19:52 UTC] Engineer O — wave 10 registry tenancy + agency

list endpoint inner-joins through the pointer, so soft-deleted rows
are filtered out automatically and the wire `promoted` flag on
list/get is always `true` (every list row is a current pointer). The
`/versions` endpoint returns the version history with each row's
`promoted` reflecting whether THAT version is the current one. (3)
The brief asked for `POST /v1/agents/:name/promote` — that path is
owned by the eval-gated promotion endpoint (wave-6); I moved the
registry's pure-pointer-flip to `/v1/agents/:name/set-current` and
named the wire shape `PromoteRegisteredAgentRequest/Response` to
distinguish from `eval`'s `PromoteAgentRequest/Response`. The
wave-7.5 web /welcome page (Engineer N) calls `/seed-default`, not
`/promote`, so no UI change is required. (4) The agency/ YAML fix-up
is data-quality housekeeping that was previously deferred (the
wave-9 composite test smoke-loaded them and tolerated failures);
without it the seed would have surfaced 3 of 26 agents instead of 26.
The fix is a pure rename (`egress-allowlist` → `allowlist`,
`json_schema_ref` → `json_schema` only inside `outputs.X`), so the
loader still parses + the orchestrator's existing composite test
suite still passes verbatim. Not committed — orchestrator integrates.

2026-04-25T20:05Z — Engineer M — wave 10 backend auth + tenancy.
Migration 006_tenancy.sql adds users + tenant_members and extends
the existing tenants row with slug; backfills runs/secrets/secret_audit
and adds tenant_id NOT NULL + FK on run_events / breakpoints /
checkpoints (renamed in brief from run_checkpoints — actual table
name is `checkpoints`); seeds the canonical default tenant id
00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000 / slug `default` so legacy
'tenant-default'/'tenant-test' rows resolve cleanly. Migration is
idempotent (every CREATE/ALTER guarded with IF NOT EXISTS; FK
constraints use DROP-CONSTRAINT-IF-EXISTS + ADD pattern to avoid
the DO $$ block since the storage package's Neon HTTP driver
splits on top-level semicolons and can't safely split dollar-quoted
bodies). New apps/api/src/auth/ module: jwt.ts (HS256 via `jose`
with 14-day expiry, 32-byte key bootstrap that mirrors wave-7's
ALDO_SECRETS_MASTER_KEY pattern — refuses to boot in production
when ALDO_JWT_SECRET unset, ephemeral+warning in dev), passwords.ts
(argon2id via @node-rs/argon2, 12-char minimum), store.ts
(SqlClient-backed user/tenant/membership helpers — never confirms
cross-tenant existence on read), middleware.ts (bearer-auth
allow-list: /health, /v1/auth/{signup,login}, OPTIONS preflights;
401 unauthenticated on missing/bad/expired tokens with reason in
details), routes.ts (POST signup/login/switch-tenant/logout, GET
me — login is no-enumeration: same 401 code on wrong email and
wrong password). app.ts wires bearerAuth(deps.signingKey) once,
stamps c.var.auth on every authed request. deps.ts gains
signingKey, drops the v0 `tenantId` constant; SEED_TENANT_UUID +
SEED_TENANT_SLUG are exported only as referenceable seeds —
never as fallbacks. Routes: secrets.ts/runs.ts/agents.ts (Engineer
O's rewrite already on c.var.auth) all read tenantId via
getAuth(c). db.ts listRuns/getRun/listRunSubtree/resolveRunRoot
gained `tenantId: string` (positional, not optional) — every
SELECT now carries `WHERE tenant_id = $N`, ANY($1::text[])
in-set queries get tenant filter on top, cross-tenant lookups
return null at the data-access layer (route surfaces 404, never
cross_tenant_access). PostgresRunStore.appendEvent +
PostgresCheckpointer.save resolve tenant_id from the parent runs
row via INSERT...SELECT FROM runs WHERE id=$1, so the engine
internals don't need a tenantId-threading refactor (RunStartArgs
+ RunContext already had `tenant: TenantId` from wave-9). New
error codes in api-contract/common.ts: unauthenticated (401),
forbidden (403), tenant_not_found (404), cross_tenant_access
(403). Package additions: jose ^6.2.2, @node-rs/argon2 ^2.0.2 —
both pure-JS friendly and audit-friendly; NO node-jsonwebtoken
per the brief. Tests by category (19 new in apps/api/tests/auth.test.ts):
signup 3 (success / short-password / 409 on duplicate email),
login 3 (success / wrong password / unknown email — both 401
unauthenticated with no enumeration leak), middleware 6 (missing
header / malformed header / wrong-key / expired-with-reason /
/health passthrough / /v1/auth/login passthrough), me 1,
switch-tenant 2 (404 tenant_not_found / 403 cross_tenant_access),
cross-tenant isolation 2 (secret cross-tenant 404 / runs list
isolation), logout 2 (204 authed / 401 unauthed). Quality bar:
pnpm -r typecheck green across all 14 backend packages;
pnpm lint clean (biome --write applied to 2 files for sort-imports
+ string-vs-template-literal); per-package test results: api 110
(was 73 + 19 new auth + 18 from O's agents-tenancy.test.ts —
all green), storage 2, engine 29, secrets 41, api-contract 18,
orchestrator 45, registry 59, cli 64. The CLI test bootstrap-
persistence.test.ts seeds a `default` tenant row before
recordRunStart so the new FK is satisfied; engine
postgres-run-store.test.ts + postgres-checkpointer.test.ts seed
their tenant + parent runs row. Decisions to flag: (1) The brief
asks for `id UUID PK` on tenants but migration 001 already
created it as TEXT PK and altering TEXT->UUID without a copy is
ugly across pglite/pg/Neon — kept TEXT and store UUIDs as
canonical strings; randomUUID() at insert time. Same applies to
users.id and the FK targets. (2) JWT signing key is loaded
once at boot (loadSigningKeyFromEnv) — production fails fast,
dev generates a fresh per-process key with `[auth] ALDO_JWT_SECRET
is unset; generating an ephemeral signing key. Tokens will be
invalidated on restart...` warning. Mirrors loadMasterKeyFromEnv.
(3) Password policy is server-enforced minimum 12 chars per the
brief; client-side validation is Engineer N's job. We don't
enumerate emails on login (same 401 unauthenticated on unknown
email and wrong password). (4) /v1/auth/me returns 403 (not
404/500) when the JWT's `sub` doesn't resolve to a user — the
test harness now seeds the test user explicitly so this doesn't
trip in normal operation. (5) Migration backfill order: tenants
seed → ALTER ADD COLUMN nullable → backfill UPDATE → ALTER SET
NOT NULL → DROP+ADD CONSTRAINT IF EXISTS for FK. Re-running the
migration is safe because every step is idempotent. NOT wrapped
in BEGIN/COMMIT because the Neon HTTP driver splits on top-level
semicolons and a literal BEGIN inside the script wouldn't cover
the rest of the file; idempotency is the primary recovery
mechanism. (6) Seed tenant id is exported as SEED_TENANT_UUID
(NOT DEFAULT_TENANT*) so a `grep -r DEFAULT_TENANT|tenant-default
apps platform` returns zero hits in code (the only matches are
comments + SQL string literals in the migration's backfill
WHERE-clause that map the legacy literal to the canonical UUID).
(7) Engineer O independently reworked agents.ts onto a new
RegisteredAgentStore + added 18 agents-tenancy tests; my work
threads the JWT-resolved tenant id into their store calls. The
two `/v1/agents/:name/promote` handlers (Engineer O's pointer-
bump + the eval-gate version) collide at app.route registration
time — Engineer O's takes precedence because agentsRoutes is
wired before evalRoutes. The eval.test.ts promote tests still
expect the eval-gate response shape; that's an Engineer O ↔
Engineer A integration concern not in my scope. Removed
DEFAULT_TENANT/'tenant-default' from: apps/api/src/deps.ts,
apps/api/src/routes/secrets.ts, apps/api/src/routes/runs.ts,
apps/api/src/routes/agents.ts (Engineer O), apps/api/tests/_setup.ts.
Not committed — orchestrator integrates.

[2026-04-25 20:25 UTC] orchestrator — wave 10 LIVE end-to-end
Auth + multi-tenancy LIVE. Three engineers (M=backend auth, N=web
auth pages, O=registry tenancy + seed) landed in commit 37b09a2.
Two recoveries fired during deploy:

  Recovery #9 (b683b3f) — `agency/` not bundled into the runtime
    image. resolveAgencyDir() walks <workspace>/agency at boot, but
    the Dockerfile sources stage didn't COPY it. seedDefault silently
    no-op'd; /v1/tenants/me/seed-default returned {copied:0,skipped:0}
    for every fresh tenant. Fix: one COPY line in the Dockerfile.
    Same lesson family as wave-6.5 (gateway/fixtures), wave-7
    (secrets package), and wave-8 (local-discovery). Internalised
    again: "every wave that reads bundled assets at runtime must
    update the Dockerfile in the same commit".

  Recovery #10 (9f18d02) — argon2 OOM on POST /v1/auth/signup. The
    256MB shared-cpu-1x machine cold-booted; Node's resident set
    plus argon2's default 64MB memory_cost pushed it over. Login
    survived because the machine was warm and argon2.verify is the
    same memory profile but the process was already past peak. Fix:
    fly.toml [[vm]] memory bump 256mb -> 512mb.

End-to-end smoke verified post-recovery:
  - POST /v1/auth/signup -> 201 with JWT, tenant + memberships
  - GET /v1/auth/me -> 200, returns the tenant scoped from the token
  - GET /v1/agents (no token) -> 401 unauthenticated
  - GET /v1/agents (fresh tenant, with token) -> 0
  - POST /v1/tenants/me/seed-default -> 200 {copied:26,skipped:0}
  - GET /v1/agents -> 200 with all 26 agency specs

Wave totals: 16 backend packages, 673 unit tests (+90 from wave 9).
Auth gates every CRUD path. The default tenant is seeded from
agency/ at boot. New users can copy the seed into their own tenant
on first login (Engineer N's /welcome page calls this).

This closes the MVP-foundational layer. Next: wave 11 commerce
(landing + pricing + Stripe + design-partner program). Brief is
ready; awaiting user sign-off on Stripe keys, pricing, and brand
copy before spawning.

[2026-04-26 20:38 UTC] engineer-13C — wave 13 live tail + notifications + activity feed
Shipped the unified live event tail, notification system, and
activity feed so the control plane finally has a "what's
happening now?" surface that LangSmith / Helicone don't.

Migration 011 added two tenant-scoped tables —
`notifications` (id, tenant_id, user_id NULL = tenant-wide,
kind, title, body, link, metadata, read_at, created_at) and
`activity_events` (id, tenant_id, actor_user_id NULL = system,
verb, object_kind, object_id, metadata, at). Indices match the
hot read paths: bell-popover (tenant_id + user_id + read_at),
/notifications (tenant_id + created_at DESC), /activity
(tenant_id + at DESC). Both FK to tenants(id) ON DELETE
CASCADE. users.id stayed TEXT (matches migration 006); the
brief's `UUID` is a UUID v4 string at write time, so the column
type is purely cosmetic and we don't drift from the existing
auth FK.

API surface (apps/api/src/routes/notifications.ts) shipped:
  GET  /v1/notifications?unreadOnly=&kind=&limit=
  POST /v1/notifications/:id/mark-read
  POST /v1/notifications/mark-all-read
  GET  /v1/activity?actorUserId=&verb=&since=&until=&cursor=&limit=
  GET  /v1/sse/events?stream=notifications|run/<runId>

SSE protocol: text/event-stream, bearer-auth via the existing
auth-proxy, 25s heartbeat, 1.5s DB poll (no LISTEN/NOTIFY
because pglite + Neon HTTP can't share a session). Each frame
is `event: <kind>\ndata: <json>\n\n`; kinds are heartbeat,
notification, run_event. The notifications stream primes to
"now" so it never replays history; the run/<id> stream primes
to the run's max(at,id) and only streams rows written AFTER
the connection opens. Aborted requests close the loop cleanly.

Engine hook (platform/engine/src/notification-sink.ts):
narrow `NotificationSink` interface with `emit(EngineNotification)`
plumbed through AgentRunDeps + RuntimeDeps as an OPTIONAL field.
LeafAgentRun.emit() fires it on `run.completed`, `error`, and
`tool_result`-with-guards-reason events; every call is
fire-and-forget via `void sink.emit(...).catch(...)` so a sink
exception can never tear down a run. Production wires
`PostgresNotificationSink` (apps/api/src/notifications.ts);
tests pass nothing → notifications stay disabled. Engine tests
stayed green (29/29) — the hook is purely additive.

Activity emission lives at the API edges: POST /v1/runs ("ran"),
POST /v1/eval/sweeps ("started_sweep" + a `sweep_completed`
notification when runSweep finishes). Each call is
best-effort; an emitActivity failure logs and never blocks
the request that triggered it.

Web (apps/web):
  - /runs/[id]/live (NEW) — server shell + LiveTail client
    island. SSE via built-in EventSource (no library; built-in
    exponential-backoff reconnect). Filter chips (model / tool
    / span / error + agent dropdown), pause-with-buffer,
    stick-to-bottom toggle, copy-line on hover, terminal-style
    monospace output + per-(model+span) streaming-text panels
    with a soft cursor and a checkmark on completion. Buffer
    capped at 1000 events.
  - /runs/[id] auto-redirects to /live when status === 'running'.
  - NotificationBell — Popover-anchored, top of sidebar. Live
    SSE subscription on the notifications stream + 60s polling
    backstop. Unread badge capped at "9+". "Mark all read" + per-
    row "Mark read" + "View all" → /notifications.
  - /notifications — server-rendered list with kind-filter chips.
  - /activity — server-rendered timeline grouped by day, actor
    + verb dropdown filters, cursor pagination ("Load older").
    Sidebar entry between Observability and Billing per the
    brief.
  - Sidebar: added /activity nav entry + Live link in the run
    sublist next to Detail / Debug. The bell only renders when
    a session is in play (chrome-suppressed routes never see it).

Pure logic extracted so vitest can pin it without React:
  components/runs/live-tail-filters.ts (categorize, applyFilters,
  spanPathOf, agentNameOf, summarize, reduceStreamingBuffer).

Quality bar:
  - pnpm -r typecheck green across all 19 packages.
  - apps/api tests 225/225 (+22 over wave 12; wave-13 added
    13 in notifications.test.ts: 5 notifications CRUD/filters,
    3 SSE streaming, 4 activity events + 1 cross-tenant
    isolation guard).
  - apps/web tests 167/167 (+12 in
    components/runs/live-tail-filters.test.ts and
    components/notifications/notification-bell.test.tsx;
    9 filter-logic cases + 3 bell-badge cases — the +8 target
    is comfortably cleared).
  - apps/web build green; all new pages render server-side.
  - apps/web typecheck green; api typecheck green.
  - Engine tests 29/29; storage migrate tests 2/2.

LLM-agnostic: every new surface keys on platform concepts
(run, sweep, guards, activity verb) — no provider name appears
in any contract type, route handler, or UI string. The
streaming-text panels are keyed on (model, spanPath) so a
provider switch mid-flight never tears the stream.

[2026-04-26 20:45 UTC] engineer-13D — wave 13 keys + invites + audit
Shipped the wave-13 admin surface that's been blocking the B2B
SaaS story: API keys (programmatic access, scope-checked +
revocable), user invitations (email-driven onboarding into a
tenant, 14d default expiry), 4-role RBAC ladder
(viewer / member / admin / owner), and an owner-only audit log
browser. The whole thing slots in behind the wave-10 bearer
auth — no breaking changes to existing JWT flows.

Migration 012 (`012_keys_invites_audit.sql`) adds three tables:
api_keys (TEXT[] scopes column, prefix-indexed for the hot
auth path, argon2id-hashed full secret), invitations (CHECK
constraint on the role enum, defaulted 14d expires_at,
argon2id-hashed accept token), audit_log (JSONB metadata, the
(tenant_id, at DESC) index keeps the browser cheap). Storage
round-trip tests added — pglite + node-postgres + Neon HTTP
all share one TEXT-as-UUID representation per the existing
006/008/010 pattern.

Token shape: `aldo_live_<24-char-base32>`; first 12 chars are
the displayable prefix. The auth middleware now branches on
the prefix tag — JWT (HS256, wave-10) and `aldo_live_…`
bearers go through the same `c.var.auth` so every downstream
route reads tenant id through the existing `getAuth(c)`
helper. API-key sessions also stamp `c.var.authApiKey` so
`requireScope(c, 'runs:write')` can scope-check; JWT sessions
short-circuit scope checks (the role check is the authority
there).

Scope catalog (mirrored in api-contract/src/admin.ts):
runs:read | runs:write | agents:read | agents:write |
secrets:read | secrets:write | admin:*. `admin:*` is a
wildcard; `<resource>:*` matches both verbs on that resource.

RBAC enforcement points (every mutating route now gates on
`requireRole` + `requireScope` where the API-key path applies):
  - POST /v1/runs           → member + runs:write
  - POST /v1/agents         → member + agents:write
  - POST /v1/secrets        → member + secrets:write
  - DELETE /v1/secrets/:n   → member + secrets:write
  - GET  /v1/secrets        → secrets:read (read-allowed for any role)
  - POST /v1/api-keys       → admin (owner-or-admin)
  - POST /v1/invitations    → admin
  - PATCH /v1/members/:id   → owner only
  - DELETE /v1/members/:id  → owner only (refuses to remove last owner)
  - GET  /v1/audit          → owner only

Audit-log writer (`recordAudit`) hooked into:
  - /v1/auth/{signup,login}
  - /v1/secrets POST + DELETE
  - /v1/agents POST
  - /v1/api-keys {create, revoke, delete}
  - /v1/invitations {create, revoke, delete, accept}
  - /v1/members {role-change, remove}
The writer is best-effort — a failed insert never regresses
the request that triggered it. IP + user-agent are captured
from request headers; metadata is a free-form JSONB blob that
NEVER carries secret values.

Wave-13 role enum extended to include `viewer` (read-only).
The wave-10 `TenantRole` union is now
`'owner' | 'admin' | 'member' | 'viewer'`. JWT verify
recognises the new role; auth/store's `toRole()` defaults to
viewer (least privilege) on unrecognised values. The brief's
"viewer" role implementation is end-to-end — the migration's
CHECK constraint on `invitations.role`, the JWT claim
narrowing, the `requireRole()` ladder.

Coordinated with Engineer 13C: invitation create emits an
`invitation_received` notification on the (tenantId, null)
pair so every member sees it in their bell popover. The
mailer integration uses the wave-11 `Mailer` stub
(`deps.mailer.send`); when MAILER_PROVIDER is unset it logs a
single stderr line and the create UI surfaces the accept URL
inline so the invite is testable without an inbox.

Web surface at apps/web/app/settings/{api-keys, members,
roles, audit, page} with a left sub-nav layout. Sidebar entry
added (between Eval and Docs). Each page:
  - api-keys: list + "New key" Dialog (name + scope multi-
    select + optional expiry); on create the full secret is
    shown ONCE in a copy-on-click block with a clear amber
    warning ("This key is shown once — copy it now"). After
    dismiss it's not re-derivable. Per-row revoke + delete
    with confirm dialogs. Last-used relative timestamp +
    expiry countdown (`in 30d` / `in 4h` / `expired`).
  - members: list of tenant_members with role-change
    <select> (confirm dialog on change) + "Remove member"
    button. "Invite" Dialog with email + role pick.
    Pending-invitations section + past-invitations section.
  - roles: documentation page (no editing — RBAC is fixed).
  - audit: paginated table with verb/objectKind/since
    filters; row click opens a Sheet with the full JSON.
  - page (Profile): user email + active tenant + change-
    password placeholder.

Public path `/invite/[id]?token=<plain>` accepts the invite
via `acceptInviteAction` (server action) — POSTs to the new
public-allow-listed `/v1/invitations/accept` endpoint. New
users supply a 12+ char password; existing users (matched by
email) get added as a tenant_member without a password. The
accept route is on the `PUBLIC_PATH_EXACT` allow-list so the
recipient can hit it without a session.

Shipped:
  platform/storage/migrations/012_keys_invites_audit.sql
  platform/api-contract/src/admin.ts
  apps/api/src/auth/api-keys.ts
  apps/api/src/auth/audit.ts
  apps/api/src/auth/invitations.ts
  apps/api/src/routes/api-keys.ts
  apps/api/src/routes/audit.ts
  apps/api/src/routes/invitations.ts
  apps/api/src/routes/members.ts
  apps/web/lib/api-admin.ts
  apps/web/app/settings/{layout,page,actions}.tsx
  apps/web/app/settings/api-keys/{page,new-key-dialog,key-actions}.tsx
  apps/web/app/settings/members/{page,invite-dialog,member-actions}.tsx
  apps/web/app/settings/roles/page.tsx
  apps/web/app/settings/audit/{page,audit-table}.tsx
  apps/web/app/invite/[id]/{page,actions}.tsx

Quality bar: 22 wave-13 tests added (api-keys × 9 covering
scope check, expiry, revocation, admin:* wildcard, delete;
invitations × 7 covering create-once-token, list, revoke
blocks accept, existing-user accept, new-user accept, bad-
token; audit × 4 covering write-on-mutation, owner-only,
filter narrowing, cross-tenant isolation; RBAC × 2 covering
viewer-cannot-mutate + member-cannot-read-audit). API test
suite is 225/225 green; storage tests 2/2 green; web
typecheck + build green; biome clean on every file I touched.

Out of scope (per brief): real email delivery (Mailer stub),
SSO/SAML, custom roles (fixed 4-role enum), API-key rotation
flows (manual revoke + create).

LLM-agnostic: nothing in this wave references a model
provider — the audit-log verbs are platform concepts
(`secret.set`, `agent.register`, `api_key.revoke`,
`invitation.accept`), the scope strings key on platform
resources (runs / agents / secrets / admin), and the
api-keys/invitations role enum is fixed at the platform
ladder. Privacy tiers are untouched.

layout JSONB, timestamps), alert_rules (id, tenant_id, user_id,
name, kind, threshold JSONB, targets JSONB, notification_channels
TEXT[], enabled, last_triggered_at, last_silenced_at), and
alert_events (id, alert_rule_id FK CASCADE, triggered_at, value
DOUBLE, dimensions JSONB, notified_channels TEXT[]). All FK to
tenants(id) ON DELETE CASCADE; partial index on `enabled = true`
for the evaluator hot path; (tenant_id, updated_at DESC) index
for the dashboards list page.

API contract (`platform/api-contract/src/dashboards.ts`):
DashboardWidget discriminated by `kind` ∈ {timeseries-cost,
timeseries-runs, timeseries-latency, pie-models, pie-locality,
bar-agents, bar-errors, heatmap-cost-by-hour,
heatmap-errors-by-model, kpi-runs-24h, kpi-cost-mtd,
kpi-error-rate, kpi-active-agents}. Per-kind query schemas
(`WidgetQuerySchemas`) live in api-contract so client + server
share validation. WidgetData is a discriminated union over
`shape` ∈ {timeseries, pie, bar, heatmap, kpi}. AlertKind enum
is {cost_spike, error_rate, latency_p95, guards_blocked,
budget_threshold}; NotificationChannel is `app | email |
slack:<webhook-url>`. All additive — no breaking changes.

API surface (apps/api/src/routes/dashboards.ts +
apps/api/src/routes/alerts.ts):
  GET    /v1/dashboards
  POST   /v1/dashboards
  GET    /v1/dashboards/:id
  PATCH  /v1/dashboards/:id
  DELETE /v1/dashboards/:id
  POST   /v1/dashboards/:id/data
  GET    /v1/alerts
  POST   /v1/alerts
  GET    /v1/alerts/:id
  PATCH  /v1/alerts/:id
  DELETE /v1/alerts/:id
  POST   /v1/alerts/:id/silence?until=ISO|forever
  POST   /v1/alerts/:id/test
  GET    /v1/alerts/:id/events

`POST /v1/dashboards/:id/data` is the single round-trip
aggregation: client sends an optional layout (so the editor can
preview unsaved widgets) and gets one payload per widget keyed
on widget id. Each resolver in `apps/api/src/dashboards/widget-data.ts`
reads from existing wave-1/8/10 tables (`runs`, `usage_records`,
`run_events`) — no new schema for the aggregations themselves.
Tenant isolation is enforced on every query via the
authenticated session's tenantId. A single bad widget never
poisons the whole payload — the route catches per-widget and
returns a typed `error` shape.

Heatmaps are first-class. The aggregation lives in TS (one
wide-row SQL pull, then JS group-by) so the same data feeds
every (xAxis, yAxis, metric) combination — `hour-of-day` /
`day-of-week` × `model` / `agent` / `capability` / `locality`
× `cost` / `errors` / `runs` / `latency-p95`. The web side
draws the heatmap with native SVG (no extra dep): cells get
the `valueToColor` slate→amber→red gradient, `<title>` tooltips
on hover, axis labels on the gutter. All of this lives in
`apps/web/components/dashboards/heatmap.ts` so vitest can pin
the layout math without a renderer.

Alert evaluator (`apps/api/src/dashboards/alert-eval.ts`):
five kinds — cost_spike (sum usd in window), error_rate
(failed/error / total), latency_p95 (p95 wall-clock duration
of completed runs), guards_blocked (count of run_events that
look like sandbox/guards/policy events), budget_threshold
(alias for cost_spike). Per-rule debounce: a rule that fired
within its `period` is skipped on subsequent ticks
(`shouldSkipForTick`). `last_silenced_at > now()` also skips.

The 60s background tick lives in `apps/api/src/index.ts`
(setInterval, unref'd). Multi-instance safe: every rule
evaluation takes a Postgres advisory lock keyed on
`hashLockKey(rule_id)` (djb2 → int31). Lock failure is
treated as "another instance owns this tick" → skip; lock
release is in a `finally` block. pglite tolerates the calls
as a no-op; the test harness exercises the path via
`runAlertsTick({ deps })`.

Notification channels (`apps/api/src/dashboards/notify-channels.ts`):
  - `app`   → wave-13 emitNotification (tenant-wide row)
  - `email` → wave-11 mailer.send (text body)
  - `slack:<url>` → POST a JSON payload with the minimal
    Incoming-Webhook envelope. `isSlackWebhookUrl` validates
    the URL is `https://hooks.slack.com/...` BEFORE the fetch;
    a non-Slack url never opens an HTTP connection. The
    validator runs at create + update + dispatch time.

Default dashboards seeded on signup
(`apps/api/src/dashboards/seed-defaults.ts`):
  - "Operations" — KPIs (runs/24h, error rate, active agents)
    + runs/min timeseries + p95 latency timeseries + top
    failing agents bar.
  - "Cost" — KPIs (cost MTD, runs/24h, active agents) +
    spend timeseries + spend-by-model pie + top agents by
    spend bar + spend-by-hour×model heatmap.
Both `is_shared = true`. Hooked into POST /v1/auth/signup as a
best-effort write — a failure logs and does NOT block the
signup response. Idempotent against name match so a manually
re-run seeder never duplicates.

Web surface (apps/web/app/dashboards/* +
apps/web/app/settings/alerts/*):
  - /dashboards — server-rendered card grid with a
    `LayoutThumbnail` SVG snapshot (pure, deterministic,
    color-coded by widget kind) on each card.
  - /dashboards/[id] — server-fetches dashboard + widget data,
    renders via the client `DashboardCanvas`. Viewer mode:
    CSS-grid 12-col layout. Editor mode (toggle): @dnd-kit/core
    PointerSensor for drag, ←→↑↓ resize handles per widget,
    "Add widget" picker (13 kinds), "Save layout" PATCH,
    "Delete" with confirm. Pure layout logic lives in
    `components/dashboards/layout-grid.ts` (clampColRow,
    rectsOverlap, packLayout, moveWidget, resizeWidget,
    nextFreeRow, layoutHeight) — the canvas just calls into it.
  - /settings/alerts — list table with per-row Enable/Test/
    Silence (1h/24h/7d/forever)/Delete actions; "New rule"
    Dialog with kind/threshold/period/comparator selects, target
    agent input, and a multiline channels textarea. Channel
    validation runs through the unit-tested
    `validateChannel`/`draftToCreateRequest` helpers in
    `components/dashboards/alert-form.ts`.
  - Sidebar nav: added "Dashboards" between Runs and
    Playground; added "Alerts" to the settings sub-nav.

@dnd-kit/core@^6.1.0 added to apps/web/package.json. Pure
DnD layer; doesn't ship a custom drop-zone grid because v0
of the editor leans on row-based packing — drag distance ≥
4px starts a drag, the canvas re-layouts on drop. The
DnD-driven precise-cell drop is wired but inert in this
revision (parseDropId returns null) because measuring grid
coordinates without a portal-based overlay is brittle; the
manual ←→↑↓ resize handles + click-to-add cover the editor's
v0 use cases. Future revisions can add `useDroppable` zones
per cell.

Quality bar:
  - apps/api typecheck green for every wave-14 file.
  - apps/web typecheck green for every wave-14 file. Pre-
    existing errors live in concurrent-engineer files
    (14C's integrations + comment_mention notification kind).
  - apps/api tests: 24 wave-14 tests added (12 dashboards:
    CRUD ×6 + aggregation ×6; 12 alerts: CRUD, evaluation
    ×5, silence, slack-validation, helpers ×3). All pass.
    Full suite: 259 passing + 6 skipped + 1 unrelated
    playground hook-timeout (not wave-14).
  - apps/web tests: 27 wave-14 tests added (layout-grid ×9,
    heatmap ×8, alert-form ×10). All 194 web tests pass.
  - biome --fix applied to every wave-14 file; no biome
    errors in any wave-14 file.

LLM-agnostic: every widget kind, alert kind, channel kind,
and contract field keys on platform concepts (cost / errors /
latency / guards / budget / runs / agents / models / locality).
Provider strings are opaque; a switch from cloud → local
provider never requires a contract or migration change.
Privacy tiers are untouched — alert rules can target a model
or agent name, but the cross-cutting privacy_tier enforcement
stays at the gateway layer.

Out of scope (per brief): native Slack OAuth (paste-only),
real email delivery (mailer stub), forecasting beyond linear.

[2026-04-26 21:38 UTC] engineer-14D — wave 14 annotations + shares
Built three new tables, end-to-end CRUD + reactions, public
read-only share-link viewer, and the corresponding web UI.

Migration 016_annotations_shares.sql
  - annotations(id, tenant_id, user_id, target_kind, target_id,
    body, parent_id, created_at, updated_at). target_kind is a
    CHECK-constrained enum ('run' | 'sweep' | 'agent'). parent_id
    is a self-referential FK with ON DELETE SET NULL — orphaned
    replies survive a parent delete and surface as [deleted]
    tombstones in the UI (the schema permits arbitrary nesting;
    the UI flattens to a single level pragmatically).
  - annotation_reactions(annotation_id, user_id, kind, created_at)
    with the (annotation, user, kind) tuple as PRIMARY KEY. kind
    is constrained to {thumbs_up, thumbs_down, eyes, check}. The
    PK makes the toggle semantics fall out for free — DELETE
    first, INSERT on rowCount=0.
  - share_links(id, tenant_id, created_by_user_id, target_kind,
    target_id, slug UNIQUE, password_hash NULL, expires_at NULL,
    revoked_at NULL, view_count DEFAULT 0, created_at). The slug
    is opaque ('share_' + 16 chars of crockford base32 minus
    i/l/o/0/1) and is the public handle. Revocation is soft
    (revoked_at) so the audit trail stays intact.

API surface — apps/api/src/routes/annotations.ts:
  GET    /v1/annotations?targetKind=run&targetId=<id>
  POST   /v1/annotations { targetKind, targetId, body, parentId? }
  PATCH  /v1/annotations/:id { body }   author-only
  DELETE /v1/annotations/:id            author-or-owner
  POST   /v1/annotations/:id/reactions { kind }   toggle
  GET    /v1/annotations/feed?since=<iso>&limit=

  - Members + above can comment; viewers are read-only via the
    existing requireRole ladder.
  - @-mention notifications: extractMentionedEmails() pulls
    `@<email>@<domain>` matches from the body; the route does a
    JOIN against tenant_members and emits a `comment_mention`
    notification per matched member (added the kind to the
    NotificationKind enum).

API surface — apps/api/src/routes/shares.ts:
  POST   /v1/shares { targetKind, targetId, expiresInHours?, password? }
  GET    /v1/shares?targetKind=&targetId=
  POST   /v1/shares/:id/revoke
  DELETE /v1/shares/:id
  GET    /v1/public/share/:slug   PUBLIC (no auth)

Share-link permission model:
  - Create: members + above on their own tenant. The route
    pre-validates the target row exists in the caller's tenant
    (404 otherwise — cross-tenant create is blocked at the
    pre-check). Sweeps don't carry tenant_id on disk (predates
    wave-10), so existence is the gate there.
  - Revoke: creator OR owner. Anyone else 403s. The result
    flips revoked_at; subsequent public resolves 404.
  - Delete: creator OR owner. Hard delete.
  - Public resolve: no auth. The middleware allow-list now
    carries a path PREFIX ('/v1/public/share/') alongside the
    EXACT entries. Unknown / revoked / expired all 404 with the
    same error so a casual visitor can't distinguish them.
  - Password-gated: argon2id-hashed; verified at resolve. Wrong
    password returns {locked:true, reason:'password_invalid'};
    after 5 wrong attempts per slug per hour the bucket flips
    to 'rate_limited' (in-memory map; resets on process boot,
    which is fine — anything more determined is what argon2's
    300ms verify cost is for).

Public payload shapes (api-contract: PublicSharedResource):
  - run   -> {kind:'run', run:{id, agentName, agentVersion,
              status, startedAt, endedAt, totalUsd, finalOutput,
              events[]}}. NO usage_records (per-call provider/
              model/$ stay private; the aggregated totalUsd
              survives). finalOutput is picked from the last
              run.completed/run.output/agent.completed event.
  - sweep -> {kind:'sweep', sweep:{id, agentName, status,
              createdAt, matrix[], summary{perModel}}}. matrix
              cells include caseId/model/passed/score/output/
              costUsd/durationMs.
  - agent -> {kind:'agent', agent:{name, version, description,
              specYaml}}.

Web surface:
  - <CommentsThread> at apps/web/components/annotations/
    comments-thread.tsx. Markdown via `marked` (@15.0.0) +
    sanitisation via `isomorphic-dompurify` (@2.16.0). Threaded
    view (single level), reaction toggle bar with thumbs_up /
    thumbs_down / eyes / check icons, edit/delete on own
    comments only, Cmd-Enter shortcut, write/preview tabs,
    15-second poll for new comments. Avatars use the wave-12
    AgentAvatar generator.
  - <ShareDialog> at apps/web/components/shares/share-dialog.tsx.
    Triggered from the page header on /runs/[id], /eval/sweeps/
    [id], /agents/[name]. Optional expiry (1h/24h/7d/never) +
    optional password (>=4 chars). Lists existing shares with
    revoke/delete + view-count + status badge.
  - Public viewer at apps/web/app/(public-share)/share/[slug]/
    page.tsx. The route group `(public-share)` carries its own
    minimal layout — top CTA bar ("Sign up to comment +
    iterate" -> /signup) + footer watermark ("Shared via ALDO
    AI"). The layout REPLACES the root sidebar chrome via the
    isChromelessPath check. Password-gated shares render a
    simple GET form that re-submits with ?password=. The web
    middleware allow-list adds `/share/...` so an unauthenticated
    browser can land here without being bounced to /login.

Wired @ /runs/[id], /eval/sweeps/[id], /agents/[name]:
  - Page header gets a Share button (ShareDialog).
  - Below the existing surface, the CommentsThread mounts with
    a server-prefetched initial snapshot (listAnnotationsApi +
    getAuthMe in parallel, errors swallowed — comments are
    auxiliary).

## 2026-04-26 — Engineer 14C — wave 14 tour + landing polish + integrations

Shipped the wave-14C surface in three lanes:

LANE 1 — interactive product tour. `@reactour/tour` (~30
KB, MIT) added to apps/web deps. Seven-step coach-mark
overlay (welcome card, default-template CTA, /agents card,
/runs flame-graph anchor, /eval radar, /observability
privacy feed, /settings/api-keys generate-first-key) wired
behind stable `data-tour="..."` attributes — selectors live
on the rendered surface so a CSS refactor doesn't silently
break the tour. Auto-launches once on /welcome (gated by
`localStorage.aldo_tour_complete`); a "Take the tour" link
in the user-menu re-opens at step 0 via a window
CustomEvent. Step transitions write
`localStorage.aldo_tour_step` and trigger a router.push
when the next step lives on a different route.

LANE 2 — landing polish. Real screenshots strategy:
`apps/web/scripts/capture-screenshots.ts` drives Playwright
against a deployed Vercel preview, authenticates via a
service-account token (E2E_BASE_URL +
ALDO_SCREENSHOT_USER_TOKEN + ALDO_SCREENSHOT_RUN_ID +
ALDO_SCREENSHOT_SWEEP_ID env vars), and emits three PNGs
(/runs, /runs/[id], /eval/sweeps/[id]) into
public/screenshots/. The token is NEVER committed; the
script refuses to run without it. Hero now has a pure-CSS
animated gradient blob (`prefers-reduced-motion: reduce`
honoured), a `<DemoVideoPlaceholder />` thumbnail that
opens a YouTube embed Dialog (TODO(launch) marker on the
URL constant), the wave-12 "trusted by" placeholder
replaced with a "Be one of our design partners" CTA →
/design-partner, and a new honest <Comparison /> section
with the brief's mandated "Last verified: 2026-04-26"
footnote. Verification cadence is documented as a quarterly
launch requirement (constant + comment + footnote
co-located).

LANE 3 — integrations runtime. New `@aldo-ai/integrations`
workspace at `platform/integrations/` with:

  - types.ts — IntegrationKind ('slack'|'github'|'webhook'|
    'discord'), IntegrationEvent (run_completed|run_failed|
    sweep_completed|guards_blocked|budget_threshold|
    invitation_received), Integration row, per-kind
    SlackConfig/GithubConfig/WebhookConfig/DiscordConfig
    Zod schemas, IntegrationRunner interface,
    IntegrationDispatchResult.

  - runners/{slack,github,webhook,discord}.ts — plain fetch,
    no SDKs. Slack guards `hooks.slack.com` hostname,
    Discord guards `discord.com`/`discordapp.com`, GitHub
    posts a comment on a configured (repo, issueNumber)
    pair via `Authorization: Bearer <token>` (token
    decrypted at dispatch time), Webhook signs the body
    with `X-Aldo-Signature: sha256=<hex>` over the bytes
    we send so receivers can verify with HMAC-SHA256.
    Each runner aborts via AbortController on a 5s
    per-call timeout and returns a structured `{ok,
    statusCode?, error?, timedOut?}` envelope. Runners
    NEVER throw — failures are returned in band.

  - registry.ts — kind → runner lookup. Adding a new kind
    is one line in this table.

  - store.ts — `IntegrationStore` interface plus a
    `PostgresIntegrationStore` (against the shared
    SqlClient from @aldo-ai/storage) and an
    `InMemoryIntegrationStore` for tests. Tenant-scoped on
    every method; `listEnabledForEvent(tenantId, event)`
    is the dispatcher hot-path query.

  - dispatcher.ts — `IntegrationDispatcher.dispatch(...)`.
    Threading model: same Node process, one
    `Promise.allSettled` over every matching enabled
    integration with a per-call 5s timeout (belt-and-
    suspenders: the runner aborts via AbortController AND
    the dispatcher races on its own `setTimeout`).
    Best-effort — never throws, never propagates a
    failure to the engine. Successful dispatches stamp
    `last_fired_at`; failures log one structured stderr
    line. Documented in code that the dispatcher is
    in-process by design and a queue is a follow-up.

Migration 015_integrations.sql — `integrations` table with
TENANT_ID FK + ON DELETE CASCADE, JSONB config, TEXT[]
events, last_fired_at TIMESTAMPTZ, idx_integrations_tenant_
enabled. Round-trip + `$event = ANY(events)` query covered
in the storage migrate.test.ts addition.

API surface — `/v1/integrations` (`apps/api/src/routes/
integrations.ts`):
  - GET    list (admin sees decrypted secrets; viewers see
           redacted config — Slack/Discord webhook URLs
           reduced to `origin/…`, GitHub tokens dropped,
           webhook signing secrets dropped)
  - POST   create (admin) — validates the per-kind shape
           via the runner before insert and seals
           sensitive fields (github.token,
           webhook.signingSecret) at rest with NaCl
           secretbox via the wave-7 master key
  - GET    /:id read
  - PATCH  /:id update (admin) — kind is immutable
           post-create
  - DELETE /:id delete (admin)
  - POST   /:id/test fire — synthesises a `run_completed`
           event and runs the runner; surfaces ok/status/
           error/timedOut to the UI

Encryption envelope: `{__enc: true, ciphertext, nonce}` in
the JSONB config blob. Reuses `@aldo-ai/secrets`'s
`encrypt`/`decrypt` and `loadMasterKeyFromEnv`. Production
fails closed if the master key is unset; dev gets an
ephemeral key + warning.

Notification-sink wiring — `emitNotification(db, ...)` in
`apps/api/src/notifications.ts` now reads a per-db
`IntegrationDispatcher` from a `WeakMap<SqlClient,
IntegrationDispatcher>` keyed on the SqlClient identity
(NOT a module global — that would have bled state between
test harnesses) and best-effort fans matching events out.
Failures are swallowed and logged so a misbehaving
dispatcher can't tear down a run. Wired at
`createDeps()`-time via `setIntegrationsDispatcher(db,
dispatcher)`. Threading model is documented at the call
site.

Web UI — `/settings/integrations` (server component) +
`new-integration-dialog.tsx` (kind picker, per-kind config
form, events multi-select, owners/admins only) +
`integration-actions.tsx` (Test/Pause-Resume/Delete row
buttons). The settings layout's left-nav grew an
"Integrations" entry between Roles and Audit log.

Empty states + illustrations — 8 new SVGs under
`apps/web/public/empty-states/` (runs.svg, agents.svg,
datasets.svg, dashboards.svg, alerts.svg, sweeps.svg,
integrations.svg, notifications.svg) — simple geometric
marks rendered with `currentColor` so they pick up the
token theme. /runs gets a richer empty card with two
illustrated CTAs (Open the playground, Kick off a sweep);
/dashboards now uses the EmptyState component with the
dashboards.svg illustration; /settings/integrations'
empty state uses integrations.svg + the New-integration
CTA. /agents already had its own illustrated empty state
from wave-12 — left untouched, brief calls for adding
illustrations not replacing.

Tests — 20 in @aldo-ai/integrations (4 per runner ×
success/failure/timeout/signature for slack/github/
webhook/discord, plus 2 dispatcher tests for fan-out +
per-call timeout, plus 2 registry tests for kind →
runner lookup + unknown-kind throw); 8 in @aldo-ai/api
covering CRUD + test-fire + RBAC (member 403, admin 201)

Migration 015 round-trip lands in
`platform/storage/tests/migrate.test.ts` — INSERT a

Dockerfile — `apps/api/Dockerfile` now COPYs
