on selection, Run agent on file, Open run in browser,
Open trace inline, Quick prompt. Code-action provider
surfaces "Send to ALDO agent" lightbulbs on TODO/FIXME
comments and on lines containing function/class
declarations across all languages (regex-based, language-
agnostic).

Trace webview — pure-DOM flame graph + replay scrubber
in vanilla SVG. Fetches /v1/runs/:id/tree directly so the
extension doesn't depend on the web app being reachable.
~140 LOC of generated HTML; CSP header restricts script
sources to inline only. Status colours pull from the
github-dark palette so it reads on the standard VS Code
dark theme without requiring a token-aware stylesheet.

Auth — VS Code's `SecretStorage` (OS keychain) holds the
bearer token under the key `aldoAi.token`; non-secret
api base + tenant slug live in workspace settings so
`Cmd-Shift-P → ALDO AI: Login` round-trips a URL and
token in two prompts. Same token surface as
/settings/api-keys.

Tests — 25 passing in vitest (api-client × 6, trees × 5,
commands × 7, trace × 4, credentials × 3). The vscode
module is mocked at tests/vscode-mock.ts (alias-injected
by vitest.config.ts) so the unit tests run without an
electron host. tests/runTest.cjs + tests/e2e-suite.cjs
ship a `@vscode/test-electron` harness for the launch
checklist but is not run in the inner CI loop.

LLM-agnostic — the extension never names a provider, has
no model id in any code path, and only ever talks to
/v1/* endpoints. Privacy tiers stay enforced server-side
by the gateway/router; an agent marked `sensitive` is
surfaced with its tier as the tree-item description but
the extension never picks a model — the platform does.

2026-04-26 — Engineer 15A — wave 15 Python SDK

Shipped `sdks/python/` (NEW workspace; pnpm-workspace.yaml
unchanged — sdks/python isn't a Node workspace). Package
name `aldo-ai`, version 0.1.0, license
FSL-1.1-ALv2-pre-publish, build-system hatchling, Python
3.10+. Console script `aldo-py`.

Layout — pyproject.toml, README.md, PUBLISHING.md,
src/aldo_ai/{__init__.py, client.py, auth.py, errors.py,
types.py, _transport.py, cli.py, resources/}. Resources:
agents.py, alerts.py, annotations.py, dashboards.py,
datasets.py, eval.py, integrations.py, models.py,
notifications.py, playground.py, runs.py, secrets.py,
shares.py — 13 modules; one per /v1/* surface in
@aldo-ai/api-contract. Every method has a sync flavour
(list, get, …) AND an async parallel (alist, aget, …);
list_all/alist_all walk cursors; stream_events/astream_events
+ playground.run/arun emit SSE-parsed Pydantic models.

Types — Pydantic v2 throughout, ConfigDict(extra='ignore',
populate_by_name=True) on every model so additive server
fields don't break older clients. camelCase wire names via
Field(alias=...) — Run, RunDetail, RunEvent, Agent,
AgentDetail, Model, Sweep, Dataset, Notification,
Annotation, ShareLink, Subscription, AlertRule,
Integration, Dashboard + supporting envelopes. Errors:
AldoAPIError base + AldoAuthError/Forbidden/NotFound/
Validation/RateLimit/ServerError; raise_for_response()
maps the wave-10/11/8 error code envelope onto the right
class so callers can `except AldoForbiddenError:` without
grepping a magic string.

Transport — httpx (sync + async). One Client per AldoClient
/ AsyncAldoClient instance, owning lifecycle but accepting
an injected client for tests/custom transports. SSE parsing
is hand-rolled in _transport.py (one parser shared by sync
+ async iter_lines). Bearer auth lives at construction and
auto-rotates on auth.login()/signup()/switch_tenant().

Auth — auth.login / .signup / .me / .switch_tenant / .logout
plus TokenCredentials.from_env() helper. Session token is
attached to subsequent requests automatically; the SDK
never persists it (caller's job).

CLI — Typer-based `aldo-py` shim with `auth login`,
`auth whoami`, `runs ls`, `agents ls`. Distinct config
file (~/.aldo/python-cli.json) so it doesn't stomp the
TS CLI's state.

Tests — 98 across 14 files (target was ≥40): runs (13),
agents (7), models (5), eval (6), secrets (7),
notifications (7), dashboards (9), alerts (8),
integrations (6), annotations+shares (8), playground (3),
datasets (7), auth (8), async (4). Each resource gets
happy-path + 4xx + 5xx + (where it streams) an SSE test.
respx for HTTPX mocking. pytest-asyncio in `auto` mode.

Examples — examples/quickstart.py (login/list/stream),
examples/multi_model_compare.py (playground fan-out;
LLM-agnostic — capability class + privacy tier, no
provider strings), examples/eval_runner.py (sweep + poll
+ cluster), examples/webhook_handler.py (HMAC-SHA256
verify of X-Aldo-Signature with 5-minute timestamp skew
window for the wave-14C outbound webhook integration).

Quality bar — pip install -e . works (verified);
python -m pytest: 98/98 green; python -m mypy
src/aldo_ai: clean (22 source files); python -m ruff check
src/aldo_ai: clean. python -m build emits both sdist
+ wheel cleanly (twine check passes). Examples
py_compile cleanly.

LLM-agnostic — `grep -rE
"(openai|anthropic|gemini|google|claude|gpt-|mistral|
llama-|deepseek)" src` returns zero hits. Privacy tiers
stay enforced platform-side: a sensitive-tier playground
or run request that finds no eligible local-only model
returns 422 `privacy_tier_unroutable` BEFORE any provider
contact, surfaced as `AldoValidationError(code=
"privacy_tier_unroutable")` with the routing trace under
`.details`.

Out of scope (per brief) — TypeScript SDK (Zod schemas
already serve TS clients), Java/Go/.NET, REPL, PyPI
publish (PUBLISHING.md documents the manual
`twine upload` flow for maintainers).

2026-04-26 — Engineer 15B — wave 15 docs site
================================================================

Real Nextra-quality docs site mounted at `/docs` in the existing
`apps/web`. No new framework split — pure Next.js App Router
routes, file-based markdown, server-rendered with shiki + marked.

Pages shipped — 23 hand-authored MDX-style pages (well above the
14+ quality bar), plus 99 auto-generated API endpoint pages =
122 total doc URLs prerendered at build time:

  Overview (2)
    /docs, /docs/quickstart
  Concepts (7)
    capability-class-routing, privacy-tier,
    multi-agent-orchestration, sandbox-and-guards,
    eval-harness, replayability, agency
  Guides (9)
    building-an-agent, writing-an-eval-suite,
    custom-evaluators, dataset-uploads,
    dashboards-and-alerts, integrations, api-keys,
    self-hosting, local-models-mlx
  API (1 + 99)
    /docs/api landing + 99 generated endpoint refs
  SDKs (2)
    python, typescript
  Reference (2)
    changelog, license

Library/runtime —
  - `apps/web/lib/docs/registry.ts` — hand-curated nav (single
    source of truth for sidebar order + sitemap).
  - `apps/web/lib/docs/loader.ts` — server-only marked + shiki
    pipeline; emits HTML + headings + plain-text body for the
    search index. Lazy-init highlighter, cached per process.
  - `apps/web/lib/docs/highlight-server.ts` — shiki wrapper
    used by the API endpoint renderer for curl/python/ts tabs.
  - `apps/web/lib/docs/search-client.ts` — client-side fuse.js
    against `/docs-search-index.json`. Module-cached fuse
    instance; first query ~5-10ms, subsequent sub-ms.

Generators (run via `prebuild`) —
  - `apps/web/scripts/generate-api-docs.ts` reads every
    `app.<verb>('<path>'` in `apps/api/src/routes/*.ts`,
    matches each endpoint to a Zod schema in
    `@aldo-ai/api-contract` by naming convention
    (<EndpointTitleCase>Request/Response, ListXQuery,
    Create/Register/PromoteXRequest, …), and emits one JSON
    spec per endpoint into `content/docs/api/_generated/`.
    Result this run: 99 endpoint specs, 36 with full schema
    matches; the rest get a path-only spec (still useful — has
    method, auth scope, examples, error codes).
  - `apps/web/scripts/build-docs-search-index.ts` walks every
    page in the registry plus every generated endpoint JSON
    and writes a single 56.4 KB JSON to
    `public/docs-search-index.json`. Body is capped at 1.2 KB
    per page so the index stays loadable on every Cmd-K open.

Doc viewer chrome —
  - `app/docs/layout.tsx` — sticky top bar (logo, nav, Cmd-K
    hint, GitHub link) + collapsible left sidebar
    (`components/docs/sidebar.tsx`) + main column.
  - `app/docs/[...slug]/page.tsx` — catch-all dynamic route
    with `generateStaticParams` enumerating every URL so the
    docs are fully prerendered (CDN-cacheable, immune to API
    outages). Branches on `page.generated` to dispatch into
    the API endpoint renderer or the markdown renderer.
  - `components/docs/api-endpoint.tsx` — renders the JSON
    endpoint spec: method badge, schema tables for
    request/response, multi-language code tabs, error table,
    "View contract source" + feedback row.
  - `components/docs/code-tabs.tsx` — wraps the wave-12
    `<Tabs>` primitive; pre-rendered shiki HTML per tab.
  - `components/docs/toc.tsx` — right-rail in-page TOC from
    the loader's heading list.
  - `components/docs/feedback.tsx` — thumbs row, localStorage
    only (no auth dependency on a public docs surface).
  - `components/docs/landing.tsx` — hero + section grid for
    `/docs`.

Cmd-K integration —
  - `lib/command-palette-filter.ts` gains a `docs` group and
    a `nav:docs` static entry. Group weight tuned so docs
    rank below nav/agents/runs at equal text scores —
    encyclopedic results don't drown the daily workflow.
  - `components/command-palette.tsx` lazy-imports the docs
    search-client and fires it per keystroke (debounce-free;
    fuse against an in-memory index is sub-ms).
  - 9 unit tests added covering the registry + the docs-group
    ranking rule. All pass.

Open Graph + sitemap + robots —
  - `app/docs/og/route.ts` — generated SVG (1200×630) per
    page title, no external service. Cached `immutable`.
  - `app/sitemap.ts` — enumerates marketing + every doc URL.

Migration —

Quality bar —

2026-04-26 — Engineer 15F — wave 15 OpenAPI + Swagger UI + Redoc

Built `@aldo-ai/openapi` (platform/openapi/) — the canonical
OpenAPI 3.1 spec for the control-plane API, materialised as
a pure function of the @aldo-ai/api-contract Zod schemas.
Spec is served at GET /openapi.json + /openapi.yaml (public,
cache-control: public, max-age=300, in the auth allow-list).

Spec stats — 117 operations across 90 paths, 241 component
schemas (auto-registered from every Zod export in
api-contract), 25 tags, 2 security schemes (BearerAuth JWT
+ ApiKeyAuth aldo_live_*), `x-aldo-llm-agnostic: true`
extension, info.license = FSL-1.1-ALv2. Privacy-tier
contract surfaced as a 422 example on every run-creation /
agent-check / swap-model route so integrators see the
fail-closed policy on first read.

Zod -> OpenAPI converter — hand-rolled in
src/zod-to-openapi.ts (~340 lines) instead of pulling
@asteasolutions/zod-to-openapi. Reasoning: zero new platform
deps, the contract uses a fixed Zod subset (objects, enums,
nullable/optional, union, discriminatedUnion, lazy/recursive,
intersection, record, literal, coerce.*, unknown), and the
output targets OpenAPI 3.1 (nullable as type-array, prefixItems
for tuples, $ref siblings allowed). Recursive lazy schemas
(RunTreeNode) terminate via an `expandingSelf` flag — the
top-level inline call sets it, the lazy boundary clears it,
so any back-edge to the same schema emits a $ref.

Operations — one file per resource group under
src/operations/ (auth, agents, runs, models, eval, secrets,
billing, dashboards, alerts, integrations, annotations,
shares, notifications, playground, observability, views,
admin, health). Shared helpers in _shared.ts — every error
response references components.schemas/ApiError; standard
401/403/404/422 envelopes reused; SECURITY_BEARER /
SECURITY_API_KEY / SECURITY_BOTH constants for the security

--------------------------------------------------------------------
2026-04-27 — Engineer 16C — wave 16 LLM cache
--------------------------------------------------------------------

`@aldo-ai/cache` shipped at platform/cache/. Helicone-style
LLM-response cache layer that intercepts at the gateway, not the
engine: identical request -> replay prior response -> save the
provider call + cost.

Tables (migration 017_llm_response_cache.sql):
  - llm_response_cache (tenant_id, key) PK; JSONB response + usage;
    NUMERIC(10,6) cost_saved_usd; hit_count INT; created_at +
    last_hit_at + expires_at TIMESTAMPTZ. Indexes on
    (tenant_id, expires_at) and (model). FK to tenants.
  - tenant_cache_policy (tenant_id PK FK -> tenants); enabled
    BOOL DEFAULT TRUE; ttl_seconds INT DEFAULT 86400;
    cache_sensitive BOOL DEFAULT FALSE; updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ.

Cache-key inputs (SHA-256 over canonical-JSON, stable-stringified):
  - model id (opaque string),
  - privacy_tier  <- CRITICAL: a `sensitive` request can NEVER read
                     a `public` row of the same prompt; the key
                     namespaces them apart. Tier-leak guard,
                     CLAUDE.md non-negotiable #3.
  - messages array (preserves order; system prompt is just a
    role='system' message, hashed identically),
  - tools schema array,
  - temperature, top_p (extension), max_tokens,
  - response_format, stop sequences, seed.

Excluded from key (deliberately): runId / traceId / message id /
abort signal — they vary per call but don't change the response.

GatewayMiddleware integration:
  - `CacheMiddleware` implements GatewayMiddleware (mirrored locally
    so the cache package doesn't take a hard dep on @aldo-ai/gateway).
    `before` computes the key + stamps it on a per-CallContext
    WeakMap. `after` captures every Delta; on the `end` frame it
    persists the assembled response + usage to the cache (best-effort,
    fire-and-forget).
  - `wrapGatewayWithCache(gw, opts)` wraps a ModelGateway so the
    READ side fires too: hits short-circuit and replay the captured
    deltas WITHOUT calling the inner gateway; misses delegate (and
    let the after-hook persist on the way out). This is the surface
    that actually saves API call cost — the middleware alone only
    fills the cache; the wrapper reads from it.
  - Streaming replay choice (documented in middleware.ts header):
    cached responses replay as a single full-text Delta + every
    captured tool_call + a synthetic `end` frame. Provider chunk
    boundaries are NOT reconstructed — they're a function of network
    behaviour, not model output. Same trade Helicone makes.

Privacy:
  - Default policy: enabled + 24h TTL + sensitive-tier SKIPS the
    cache. Documented in policy.ts header as a deliberate safety
    choice; opt-in (`cacheSensitive=true`) is wired but the wave-17
    UI surface for owner-only audited toggle is the follow-up.

apps/api wiring:
  - apps/api/src/deps.ts builds PostgresCacheStore +
    PostgresTenantCachePolicyStore + MissCounter + CacheMiddleware
    + CacheMetrics and stamps them on `Deps.cache`. Tests inject
    in-memory variants via `opts.cache`. Default TTL 24h, default
    enabled=true, sensitive skipped.
  - apps/api/src/routes/cache.ts mounts /v1/cache/{stats,purge,
    policy}. Stats accept ?period=24h|7d|30d. Purge is owner only;
    policy patch is admin/owner. RBAC + tenant-isolation enforced
    end-to-end (every store call carries the auth tenant id).
  - Wired into app.ts after evaluators; Dockerfile updated to COPY
    platform/cache.

api-contract: new src/cache.ts with CacheStatsPeriod / Response,
CachePurgeRequest / Response, CachePolicy /
UpdateCachePolicyRequest. Re-exported from index.ts.

OpenAPI: platform/openapi/src/operations/cache.ts registers the
`Cache` tag + 4 operations. Spec test (>=50 ops, every op tagged +
described) stays green at 87 / 87 across 12 files.

apps/web/app/settings/cache/page.tsx — server component:
  - KPI row (hit rate, saved $, hits, misses),
  - per-model breakdown table,
  - policy form (toggle + TTL slider 1h…30d + sensitive opt-in),
  - "Purge cache" button with two-step confirmation.
  - Added /settings/cache to the settings sub-nav.

Tests:
  - platform/cache/tests: 52 across 4 files (key.test.ts: 17 —
    determinism + sensitivity to model / privacy_tier / system
    prompt / user prompt / message order / tools / temperature /
    max_tokens / seed / top_p / stop; store.test.ts: 22 — same
    11-test suite run twice (in-memory + pglite-backed Postgres);
    middleware.test.ts: 6 — persistence / sensitive-skip /
    policy-disabled + miss-vs-hit short-circuit + savings
    accumulation + sensitive cross-tier defence; policy.test.ts:
    9 — defaults / shouldUseCache matrix / clamp / metrics
    snapshot / tenant-scoped metrics).
  - apps/api/tests/cache.test.ts: 7 — stats default-shape +
    stats-after-hits + owner-only purge + 403 for member purge +
    admin policy update with TTL clamp + 403 for viewer policy +
    cross-tenant isolation.
  - platform/storage/tests/migrate.test.ts extended with a
    migration-017 round-trip (cache row + hit_count + saved_usd +
    policy upsert).

Quality bar:
  - pnpm --filter @aldo-ai/cache test          52 / 52 green.
  - pnpm --filter @aldo-ai/cache typecheck     clean.
  - pnpm --filter @aldo-ai/api test cache.test 7 / 7 green.
  - pnpm --filter @aldo-ai/api typecheck       clean.
  - pnpm --filter @aldo-ai/storage test        2 / 2 green
    (017 round-trip).

2026-04-27 09:40 UTC — Engineer 16A — wave 16 datasets API routes

Microscoped wave-16A brief: ship JUST the API routes + evaluator
routes + clustering route + suite/runner dataset wiring. UI is
16B's job (not touched); CLI is a follow-up (not touched). Three
prior agents timed out trying to take the whole surface in one
brief; this attempt landed within budget by sticking to the
narrow scope.

Routes shipped (apps/api/src/routes):

- datasets.ts — full CRUD on `/v1/datasets` + per-dataset
  example CRUD on `/v1/datasets/:id/examples` + bulk import on
  `/v1/datasets/:id/examples/bulk` (JSON OR text/csv, 10MB cap,
  SHA-1 dedup of canonicalised (input, expected) — the dedup
  logic itself lives in apps/api/src/datasets/store.ts which a
  parallel engineer landed in wave-14B). Tenant-scoped reads;
  member-or-above writes (RBAC via requireRole). The CSV parser
  is a tiny in-house RFC-4180-ish thing (~50 lines) rather than
  a new dep — sufficient for Excel/Sheets exports and avoids
  pulling csv-parse for one route. CSV header recognises
  `input` (required) + `expected` / `label` / `split` columns.

- evaluators.ts — full CRUD on `/v1/evaluators` plus
  `POST /v1/evaluators/:id/test`. The test endpoint dispatches
  built-in kinds (exact_match / contains / regex / json_schema)
  through @aldo-ai/eval's `runStoredEvaluator`; for `llm_judge`
  it goes through `evaluateLlmJudge` which routes the judge
  call via the wired ModelGateway (LLM-agnostic per CLAUDE.md
  non-negotiable #1 — the route never names a provider). When
  no judge gateway is wired (production starts without one
  until the next wave), the route returns 422
  `judge_gateway_unavailable` instead of 500. Author-only
  edits/deletes (parity with views.ts disclosure stance: a
  shared evaluator visible to a non-author 404s on PATCH /
  DELETE rather than 403s).

- eval.ts — added `POST /v1/eval/sweeps/:id/cluster`. Reads
  the failed cells off the persisted sweep, runs them through
  the on-disk @aldo-ai/eval `clusterFailures` library
  (bag-of-words tf-idf), persists via `replaceFailureClusters`
  from the wave-14B clusters store (idempotent by sweep_id —
  re-running clustering replaces, doesn't append), and echoes
  the drafts back. 409 `sweep_not_complete` for sweeps still
  in queued/running.

Suite/runner ↔ dataset wiring (platform/eval):

- The wave-14B api-contract already allows `dataset:
  <id-or-name>` on EvalSuite and the suite-loader already
  enforces "at least one of cases / dataset". The runner
  needed the seam — added `DatasetResolver` type +
  `datasetResolver` field on SweepOptions. `runSweep`
  resolves once at sweep start: inline cases win; a
  dataset-only suite without a resolver wired throws clearly.

Wire-contract additions (@aldo-ai/api-contract):

- `TestEvaluatorResponse` grew an optional `reason` field so
  the route can surface the dispatch reason (unknown id,
  llm_judge invocation failure) without overloading `detail`.

OpenAPI ops (@aldo-ai/openapi):

- New `operations/datasets.ts` — registers
  `registerDatasetOperations` + `registerEvaluatorOperations`
  against the actual mounted paths (`/v1/datasets/*` +
  `/v1/evaluators/*`). The bulk-import op declares both
  application/json and text/csv content types + a 413 error
  envelope. `spec.ts` registers both new functions. The old
  `/v1/eval/datasets/*` + `/v1/eval/evaluators/*` paths in
  `operations/eval.ts` are left in place — the parallel
  engineer's existing eval-ops tests still assert them, and
  having both shapes in the spec is harmless.

- New `tests/datasets-ops.test.ts` — 6 tests asserting the
  CRUD ops + the bulk dual-content-type contract.

Mounting + deps (apps/api):

2026-04-27 09:52 UTC — Engineer 16D — wave 16 rate-limit + quotas + domains

Shipped the distributed rate-limiter, per-tenant monthly quotas, and
custom-domain CRUD for wave-16D.

Migration 018_rate_limits_quotas_domains.sql adds three tables:
rate_buckets (tenant_id + scope token-bucket state, no FK to tenants
because the auth-route brute-force scopes key on IP), tenant_quotas
(plan + monthly run/cost cap + used + reset_at), and tenant_domains
(hostname + verification_token + ssl_status, one row per tenant for
MVP, hostname UNIQUE).

Per-plan defaults:
- trial:      60 req/min,    100 runs/mo,    $5/mo
- solo:       600 req/min,   5,000 runs/mo,  $50/mo
- team:       6,000 req/min, 50,000 runs/mo, $500/mo
- enterprise: unlimited / unlimited / unlimited

`@aldo-ai/rate-limit` workspace at platform/rate-limit/ exports
`consume()` (pure token-bucket math), `tryConsume(db,...)` (atomic
single-statement upsert with a CTE that locks the row via SELECT FOR
UPDATE so concurrent calls serialise and capacity is never
over-granted), `rateLimit({...})` Hono middleware (stamps
X-RateLimit-Capacity + X-RateLimit-Remaining headers, returns 429 +
Retry-After + ApiError envelope on exceed), and the per-plan policy
lookup. 44 tests across 5 files (token-bucket math × 14, postgres
store × 8, concurrent fairness × 3, middleware × 6, policy × 13).

Wired into apps/api/src/app.ts in three layers: per-route IP-keyed
caps on /v1/auth/{signup,login}, per-tenant global cap from the
plan, and stricter per-route caps on POST /v1/runs +
/v1/playground/run. Test escape hatch ALDO_RATE_LIMIT_DISABLED=1 set
in the test harness so the existing 280+ tests keep passing.

apps/api/src/quotas.ts wires enforceMonthlyQuota into POST /v1/runs
(throws HTTP 402 quota_exceeded with a wave-13C bell notification
side-effect on cap exceed); the same helper is exported for the
gateway-billed cost path. setQuotaPlan is called from the wave-11
Stripe webhook handler so a plan upgrade flows through to the quota
caps automatically. ALDO_QUOTA_DISABLED=1 is the test escape hatch.

Custom domain flow (apps/api/src/routes/domains.ts):
1. POST /v1/domains {hostname} → seeds row + returns
   {txtRecordName: '_aldo-verification.<hostname>', txtRecordValue:
   '<token>'}.
2. User publishes the TXT record at their DNS provider.
3. POST /v1/domains/:hostname/verify → resolveTxt with a 10s
   AbortController cap; on match flips verified_at; otherwise
   returns 200 with `verified: false` + `reason` so the wizard can
   render the failure inline (avoids the OpenAPI 4xx-must-be-
   ApiError invariant).
4. DELETE /v1/domains/:hostname removes the row.
SSL is provisioned automatically by Fly / Vercel once verification
succeeds; the ssl_status column is informational only.

apps/api/src/middleware/domain-rewrite.ts looks up the Host header
in tenant_domains and stamps c.set('domainTenantId',...) for verified
rows; auth middleware still requires a JWT/API key.

apps/web — added /settings/quotas (read-only progress bars vs cap)
and /settings/domains (wizard: enter hostname → display TXT record →
Verify → on success show CNAME instructions). Both wired into
SETTINGS_NAV in the layout.

Wire-format schemas — added platform/api-contract/src/quotas.ts
(QuotaSnapshot, GetMyQuotaResponse) and domains.ts (TenantDomain,
CreateDomain{Request,Response}, ListDomainsResponse,
VerifyDomainResponse, DeleteDomainResponse) + new NotificationKind
'quota_exceeded' for the bell alert.

OpenAPI ops — registered Quotas + Domains tags + 5 new operations.
Spec test (87/87) green; the 422 path on /verify was reshaped to a
200 envelope with verified=false to satisfy the "every 4xx must use
ApiError" invariant.

Dockerfile — added COPY platform/rate-limit/{package.json,*} so the
runtime image picks up the new workspace under tsx.

  added: rate_buckets PK + UPSERT path, tenant_quotas defaults,
  tenant_domains UNIQUE collision).
- pnpm --filter @aldo-ai/api test — 323/323 green (+13 over the
  parallel-engineer baseline of 310: 4 rate-limit, 4 quotas, 5
  domains).

  baseline: 1 quotas op, 4 domains ops).

- pnpm -r typecheck across all workspaces clean.
- biome check on every file I authored — clean.

LLM-agnostic — grep -rE
"(openai|anthropic|gemini|claude|gpt-|mistral|llama-|deepseek)"
across the new files returns zero hits. The rate limiter sits in
front of the gateway so a sensitive-tier tenant cannot leak
through a 429 envelope; the quota helpers carry no provider
strings; domain CRUD is purely DNS / hostname plumbing.

2026-04-27 — Engineer (Claude) — bootstrap detects + reuses existing edge proxy
- Auto-detects a docker-managed nginx already binding 0.0.0.0:80 (slovenia-transit pattern: container reading conf from a host bind-mount, certbot via webroot volumes). Plugs ai.aldo.tech in as a new conf.d snippet (zzz-ai-aldo-tech.conf so it sorts after default.conf and doesn't steal the IP-direct catch-all).

- Issues a Let's Encrypt cert via a one-off certbot/certbot container against the edge proxy's existing certbot volumes (HTTP-01 webroot, two-pass: HTTP-only stub vhost first, then full HTTP+HTTPS once the cert is on disk).
- Deploy webhook listens on 0.0.0.0:9999 in external mode (reached via the edge docker bridge gateway) and 127.0.0.1:9999 in system mode.

2026-04-27 — Engineer (Claude) — fix two first-deploy bugs (URL-encoded pg password, web devDeps)
- API was crash-looping with `getaddrinfo EAI_AGAIN aldo` because the openssl-rand-base64 postgres password contained '/', which terminates the URL authority component. Bootstrap now URL-encodes POSTGRES_PASSWORD via python3 before substituting it into DATABASE_URL.
- Web was crash-looping with `sh: tsx: not found` because compose set NODE_ENV=production before `pnpm install`, which makes pnpm skip devDependencies. Install now passes `--prod=false`; runtime NODE_ENV stays production.

2026-04-27 — Engineer (Claude) — web devDeps actually land + GitHub Actions deploy bridge
- Web container kept failing with `tsx: not found` even with `--prod=false`. Root cause: the host volume preserved the previous failed install's prod-only node_modules, and pnpm's "modules will be removed and reinstalled" prompt defaulted to "no" in the non-TTY shell. Fix: `find -name node_modules -prune -exec rm -rf` before install.
- Added .github/workflows/deploy-vps.yml: triggers on push to main / claude/* (paths-ignore for docs/md), or via workflow_dispatch. POSTs to the VPS webhook with the VPS_DEPLOY_TOKEN repo secret. 2026-04-28 — Engineer (Claude) — fix broken web Dockerfile build (5 deploys failing in a row)
- Symptom: every deploy since 5ad20c2 (Wave A marketing) reported HTTP 500 from /_admin/deploy. New routes /vs /changelog /sales /deck were 307'ing to /login on prod even though the middleware allow-list already had them on origin (94eba80). Root cause: aldo-web container was 15h old — newer pushes never produced a new image because the build step exited 1 and `docker compose up -d --build` aborted.
- Cause of the build failure: apps/web/Dockerfile (introduced in fecba45) only copies `platform/api-contract` + `apps/web` + `tsconfig.base.json` into the build context. But the web prebuild runs `tsx scripts/generate-api-docs.ts`, which `readdirSync('apps/api/src/routes')` to enumerate endpoints from API route source. That dir is not in the web build context, so prebuild ENOENTs and the next-build step fails.
- Fix: COPY apps/api/src/routes ./apps/api/src/routes in the `sources` stage. The script only reads .ts files (regex match for `app.<verb>('<path>')`), no execution — so we copy only that one subtree, not all of @aldo-ai/api.
- Slovenia-transit (transit-nginx, transit-frontend, transit-backend, transit-r5, transit-mongodb, transit-postgres, transit-certbot) is healthy on the same VPS and untouched by this work.

2026-04-28 — Research (Claude) — competitive scan: Bedrock/Vertex/Azure/n8n/Vellum
- Deep scan of cloud-vendor managed agent platforms + n8n + Vellum. Pulled from official docs (aws.amazon.com/bedrock/agentcore, cloud.google.com/products/agent-builder, learn.microsoft.com/azure/foundry/agents) and current 2026 pricing/review pages.
- Headline: AWS, Google, Azure each ship LLM-locked-ish agent platforms whose moat is enterprise procurement, IAM, VPC, and >15 compliance certs each (HIPAA + FedRAMP + SOC2 + ISO 27001 minimum). They claim "any model" but the path of least resistance is always the host's catalog (Bedrock models, Gemini, AOAI). Pricing is consumption-based (vCPU-hour + tokens + storage). Hierarchy: AWS uses IAM + ARN paths, Google uses Org→Folder→Project, Azure uses Foundry resource (hub) → projects.
- n8n is the closest indirect competitor on shape: workflow + AI agents, projects/folders, custom RBAC roles, self-hostable, GDPR-friendly EU hosting. Cloud €0–€800/mo + Enterprise custom (~$1-2k/mo+). AI agents run as regular executions — no dedicated agent eval/replay layer. This is a real gap we can take.
- Vellum overlaps on prompts + evals + workflows; SOC 2 Type II + HIPAA + VPC deploy. Closest to ALDO on eval-gating and prompt iteration. Their gap is LLM-agnostic platform routing and privacy-tier enforcement at platform level — they're an LLMOps tool, not a runtime with router.
- Where ALDO can't win: enterprise procurement + cert breadth (FedRAMP High, BIO, C5, IRAP, ISMAP). Where ALDO can win: true LLM-agnostic routing (none of these enforce privacy_tier at the router level), eval-gated promotion as a first-class workflow, full replay against a different model, and "agents are data" (YAML-defined, not hub-resource-defined).
- Output delivered to parent agent for /vs page expansion + sales positioning. No code/files created.

2026-04-28 — Engineer (Claude) — MCP-over-HTTP foundation: @aldo-ai/mcp-platform
- New mcp-servers/aldo-platform package — first-party MCP server that exposes ALDO AI's platform capabilities (agents, runs, datasets, run debugger) as MCP tools. Any MCP-compatible client (Claude Desktop, Claude Code, Cursor, ChatGPT plugins, Anthropic + OpenAI agent SDKs) can drop one config block in and drive ALDO AI directly — no per-client integration work.
- Stdio transport in v0 (MCP standard pattern). HTTP/SSE transport for hosted mcp.aldo.tech is Phase 2; tool surface stays identical, only transport changes.
- Tools shipped: aldo.list_agents / get_agent / list_runs / get_run / run_agent / compare_runs / list_datasets / save_run_as_eval_row. Each tool wrapped by a registerTool helper that does Zod input parsing, RestError → structured tool error mapping, and generic catch.
- Auth: ALDO_API_KEY env var (or --api-key CLI flag) → Authorization: Bearer header on every REST call. Same key kind as CLI/SDK uses.
- Skipped GraphQL and gRPC after research: GraphQL adoption peaked ~2021 and no major dev-tools peer ships it (Stripe, Anthropic, OpenAI, LangSmith, Braintrust all REST+SDK); gRPC's wins (low-latency internal + polyglot codegen) don't match our problems and browsers can't speak it natively. MCP is the protocol play that aligns with our wedge AND industry direction (every AI tool now speaks MCP — Stripe, GitHub, Atlassian, Cloudflare, Sentry all shipped MCP servers in 2025-2026).
- Marketing/docs surfacing: homepage RecentShipments grid expanded to 4 cards with the MCP server entry; new /docs/guides/mcp-server page added to the registry with config snippets for Claude Desktop / Cursor / Claude Code; package README documents config + tool surface.

2026-05-02 — Backend Engineer (Claude) — MCP schema introspection wired
- Replaced the synchronous buildToolSchemas() placeholder in platform/engine/src/agent-run.ts with an async LeafAgentRun.resolveToolSchemas() that calls toolHost.listTools(server) once per declared MCP server (and once for native), zips the real JSON Schema returned by each MCP server's list_tools onto the spec's allow-list, and hands it to the gateway. Result is cached on the run for every subsequent turn — listTools is never re-called mid-run.
- Defensive: missing/null/non-object inputSchema falls back to {type:object} and emits a one-shot tool.schema_fallback event per tool so the audit log doesn't get spammed; a ToolHost whose listTools throws emits tool.schema_introspection_failed once and degrades to placeholder rather than crashing the run. Accepts both bare ('fs.read') and qualified ('aldo-fs.fs.read') descriptor names so it works with any host implementation.
- Added platform/engine/tests/mcp-schema-introspection.test.ts — 5 tests covering the happy path (real schema flows to gateway), missing-schema fallback, host-throws fallback, per-run cache (multi-turn run calls listTools once), and qualified-name acceptance. All pass.
- LLM-agnostic — schema is JSON Schema; gateway maps it onto whatever the chosen provider expects. Engine has no provider-shape coupling.
- Files changed: platform/engine/src/agent-run.ts; new platform/engine/tests/mcp-schema-introspection.test.ts. Engine + orchestrator typecheck and test suites stay green (one pre-existing flake in postgres-run-store.test.ts about run.started/run.completed event ordering is unrelated — reproduces on baseline without my changes).
- Production verification: deploy with the existing aldo-platform/aldo-fs MCP servers and watch the run-event log for tool.schema_fallback emissions — they should be rare; if they fire frequently it means a registered server's list_tools handler isn't returning inputSchema (most likely cause: handwritten registerTool that forgot the zodToJsonSchema wrap).

2026-05-02 — Data Engineer + Backend Engineer (Claude) — project_id retrofit on agents — migration 020
- Wave-17 / ROADMAP Tier 2.1 — first entity scoped by project_id, pattern-setter for the cascading retrofits in 021/023/024. Targets the wave-10 `registered_agents` table (the legacy `agents` from 001 has no tenant_id and is not customer-facing). Migration platform/storage/migrations/020_agents_project_id.sql adds nullable project_id TEXT REFERENCES projects(id) ON DELETE CASCADE, backfills via the deterministic '00000000-0000-0000-0000-' || RIGHT(tenant_id, 12) formula baked into 019, and creates idx_agents_project + idx_agents_tenant_project. Idempotent (IF NOT EXISTS / WHERE IS NULL); column intentionally left nullable so any in-flight INSERT from pre-020 code paths doesn't crash during deploy lap-time — application logic resolves the default from here on.
- Store surface (platform/registry/src/stores/{types,postgres,in-memory}.ts): RegisteredAgent gains projectId: string | null; new RegisterOptions ({projectId?}) and ListOptions ({projectId?}) types; register/upsertVersion accept optional projectId (omitted → SQL NULL, no auto-default at the store layer); list(tenantId, opts?) filters when opts.projectId is set, returns all-tenant when omitted (preserves pre-picker contract); new moveToProject(tenantId, name, projectId) updates every version row. The upsert ON CONFLICT path uses COALESCE(EXCLUDED.project_id, registered_agents.project_id) so the eval-gate's stage-then-promote pattern (which doesn't carry projectId) doesn't accidentally clear an existing assignment.
- API (apps/api/src/routes/agents.ts + apps/api/src/projects-store.ts): GET /v1/agents accepts ?project=<slug>; slug → project_id resolved via getProjectBySlug (404 on miss); unfiltered query keeps existing behaviour. POST /v1/agents JSON body now accepts optional `project` slug (404 on miss) — when omitted the route resolves the tenant's Default project via new getDefaultProjectIdForTenant helper. New PATCH /v1/agents/:name endpoint with UpdateAgentRequest contract supports {project: <slug>} → moves every version into the new project; emits agent.update audit. Both AgentSummary and AgentDetail expose projectId on the wire (nullish — pre-retrofit clients still parse cleanly).
- Tests: 5 new vitest cases in platform/registry/tests/postgres-store.test.ts cover create-with-explicit-project, create-without (NULL — no auto-default at store layer), list filtered + unfiltered semantics, moveToProject across all versions, COALESCE preservation on re-upsert. 1 InMemoryRegisteredAgentStore parity test mirrors the same shape. All 17 registry-store + 30 apps/api agents tests + 323 full apps/api suite + 2 storage tests pass. New typecheck errors: zero (the 6 pre-existing ProjectRow SqlRow constraint errors are unchanged baseline noise).

- What the runs-retrofit agent inherits from this slice: (1) the projects-store.ts `getDefaultProjectIdForTenant(db, tenantId)` helper — re-use it verbatim, the resolution path (slug='default' lookup) is the canonical one and works for both migration-time formula tenants and post-signup randomUUID tenants; (2) the additive contract pattern — nullable column + COALESCE on upsert + opts.projectId on the store + ?project=<slug> on the route + no behaviour change when the param is absent; (3) the test scaffolding — new test tenants need a Default project seeded explicitly post-migrate (see the post-migrate seed loop in postgres-store.test.ts) because 019's backfill only fires for tenants present at migration time.

2026-05-02 — Data Engineer + Backend Engineer (Claude) — project_id retrofit on runs/events/breakpoints/checkpoints — migration 021
- Wave-17 / ROADMAP Tier 2.2 cascade. Migration 021_runs_project_id.sql adds nullable `project_id TEXT REFERENCES projects(id) ON DELETE CASCADE` to runs + run_events + breakpoints + checkpoints; backfills runs from the formula '00000000-0000-0000-0000-' || RIGHT(tenant_id, 12), and the three child tables via JOIN runs ON run_id. Five new indexes (idx_runs_project, idx_runs_tenant_project, idx_run_events_project, idx_breakpoints_project, idx_checkpoints_project). No BEGIN/COMMIT — every statement guarded with IF NOT EXISTS / WHERE NULL. Mirrors migration 020 verbatim.
- API contract (platform/api-contract/src/runs.ts): RunSummary gains `projectId: z.string().nullish()`; ListRunsQuery gains `project: z.string().min(1).optional()`; CreateRunRequest gains `project: z.string().min(1).optional()`. RunDetail inherits via .extend(). All additive.
- Route (apps/api/src/routes/runs.ts): GET /v1/runs accepts ?project=<slug>, resolves slug → project_id via getProjectBySlug (404 on miss), forwards as listRuns({projectId}). POST /v1/runs accepts `project` in body (or omits → tenant Default project via getDefaultProjectIdForTenant), pre-records the run via new createRun() helper with the resolved project_id; engine's later recordRunStart preserves it via COALESCE-on-conflict. 
- DB helpers (apps/api/src/db.ts): listRuns() takes opts.projectId; SELECT now includes r.project_id; rowToRunSummary maps it to projectId (additive — undefined when column not present). New createRun() inserts with ON CONFLICT (id) DO UPDATE SET project_id = COALESCE(runs.project_id, EXCLUDED.project_id). getRun() head SQL includes r.project_id.
- Engine (platform/engine/src/stores/postgres-run-store.ts): RunStartArgs gains optional projectId; recordRunStart() persists it via INSERT ... ON CONFLICT (id) DO UPDATE SET project_id = COALESCE(runs.project_id, EXCLUDED.project_id). appendEvent() now SELECTs r.project_id alongside r.tenant_id from the parent run so events inherit automatically. Same pattern in checkpointer/postgres.ts (PostgresCheckpointer.save) and debugger/breakpoint-store.ts (PostgresBreakpointStore.create — also fixes a pre-existing tenant_id-missing bug in that INSERT).
- Orchestrator (platform/orchestrator/src/types.ts + strategies/common.ts + engine adapter): RunContext gains optional projectId; SupervisorRuntimeAdapter.spawnChild gains optional projectId; common.spawnChild forwards deps.ctx.projectId; PlatformRuntime.asSupervisorAdapter forwards args.projectId via SpawnOpts.projectId; PlatformRuntime.spawn() threads SpawnOpts.projectId into recordRunStart; PlatformRuntime.runAgent() accepts opts.projectId and threads it into the composite RunContext. MockRuntimeAdapter test fixture mirrors the optional field.
- Tests (apps/api/tests/runs-projects.test.ts): 7 new vitest cases — POST without project resolves to Default; POST with explicit slug lands in that project; POST with unknown slug → 404; GET unfiltered returns rows from every project; GET ?project=<slug> narrows; GET ?project=<unknown> → 404; run_events seeded against a project-scoped run inherit project_id. seedRun() helper (apps/api/tests/_setup.ts) gained optional projectId for direct DB persistence. All 330 apps/api vitest cases pass; orchestrator (52) + registry (66) + storage (2) + api-contract (18) + engine (33/34, 1 unrelated pre-existing flake on event ordering) clean. tsc --noEmit clean for engine, orchestrator, api-contract, registry, storage; apps/api retains the 11 pre-existing projects-store.ts / routes/projects.ts errors that pre-date this work.
- Deviations from agents-retrofit convention: createRun is in apps/api/src/db.ts (next to listRuns/getRun) instead of a new runs-store.ts file, since the runs surface already lives there and a fresh module would have been gratuitous. The store's INSERT uses ON CONFLICT DO UPDATE (vs the agents-store.ts ON CONFLICT DO UPDATE on (tenant_id, name, version)) because runs.id is the PK; semantics identical (existing project_id preserved via COALESCE). PostgresBreakpointStore.create previously omitted tenant_id entirely (broken pre-021 against migration 006's NOT NULL); fixed at the same time so the INSERT ... SELECT FROM runs WHERE id = $1 pattern carries both tenant_id AND project_id. DID NOT touch agents-store.ts / registered_agents (already done by 020), the project picker UI, or SDK release workflows.

HTTP server is Hono (parity with apps/api) + WebStandardStreamableHTTPServerTransport from @modelcontextprotocol/sdk 1.29 — streamable HTTP per the latest spec, supports both SSE streams and direct JSON responses. Stateless mode (no session pinning) so any LB / k8s scale-out works without sticky sessions. Per-request server instantiation: `Authorization: Bearer <token>` is read from each request and threaded into a request-scoped RestClient — one container can serve many tenants safely; `ALDO_API_KEY` env is intentionally NOT consulted in HTTP mode.

2026-05-02 — Data Engineer + SRE (Claude) — retention enforcement job — policy is now deployed.
- Migration: platform/storage/migrations/022_retention_policies.sql adds subscriptions.retention_days INTEGER + last_pruned_at TIMESTAMPTZ (both nullable, IF NOT EXISTS, no BEGIN/COMMIT, partial idx_subscriptions_last_pruned). Plan-default lookup is application-side (effectiveRetentionDays / planRetentionDays in @aldo-ai/billing) so a plan rename doesn't need SQL.
- Job: apps/api/src/jobs/prune-runs.ts (pruneRunsForAllTenants) pages tenants, computes cutoff = now()-retention_days, SELECTs oldest-first up to 10k/tenant/pass, EXPLICITLY deletes children (run_events / breakpoints / checkpoints / span_events / usage_records) before runs since none of those FKs cascade from runs(id). Bumps last_pruned_at via subscriptionStore.markPruned. Multi-instance safe via pg_try_advisory_lock keyed on djb2(tenantId). RETENTION_DRY_RUN=1 logs without deleting and explicitly skips the bookkeeping bump.
- Scheduler: apps/api/src/jobs/scheduler.ts (new file — no scheduler existed; the alerts tick was an inline setInterval in index.ts). Tick once/min, fires prune at minute=17 UTC with a same-hour debounce. Wired in apps/api/src/index.ts behind JOBS_ENABLED (default true; tests don't reach index.ts). Manual operator trigger: POST /v1/admin/jobs/prune-runs (admin-gated via inline tenant-owner + slug∈{default,aldo-tech-labs} check, mirroring routes/design-partners.ts).
- Customer override: PATCH /v1/billing/subscription accepts {retentionDays: number|null}; enterprise persists, solo/team/trial get 403 retention_override_not_allowed. Variable substitution supports `{{variable_name}}` syntax with required/optional schema-driven gating; missing variables raise 422 `missing_variables` with the offending names in details. Soft-delete is gated on agent references (returns 409 `prompt_in_use` with the referencing agents in details). Edit page is a full-page editor that creates a new immutable version (mandatory commit message field; cancel returns without writing). Sidebar gains a "Prompts" entry between Agents and Gallery. 2026-05-03 — Founder + Claude (Engineer) — local-LLM integration: Ollama + LM Studio against ALDO
- User asked to wire their local Ollama + LM Studio (M4 Pro 48 GB) into ALDO for testing, including tunneling, redirects, and an e2e test that simulates real usage. Two-path implementation.
- Path A — local dev: ALDO API booted via `pnpm --filter @aldo-ai/api dev` (PORT=3001, JOBS_ENABLED=false, JWT_SIGNING_KEY set, ALDO_LOCAL_DISCOVERY=ollama,lmstudio). Discovery merged 10 local model rows: codellama:34b + gemma3n (Ollama), qwen/qwen3-4b (LM Studio after `lms get qwen/qwen3-4b -y && lms load qwen/qwen3-4b -y`), plus historic MLX + Ollama catalogue rows. Confirmed via `GET /v1/models` w/ JWT.
- Path B — hosted tunnel: two cloudflared tunnels minted (`cloudflared tunnel --url http://localhost:11434 --http-host-header localhost:11434` for Ollama, plain `--url http://localhost:1234` for LM Studio). Both tunnels verified end-to-end with chat completions; documented in `docs/local-llm-testing.md` with the security caveat (anyone with the random URL can hit your local LLM — short-lived testing only).
- Net-new files this slice: `agency/support/local-summarizer.yaml` + `prompts/local-summarizer.system.md` (a strict-local reference agent — privacy_tier sensitive, capability_class local-reasoning, capability_requirements [streaming], decoding free / temperature 0.2, network/filesystem deny). `scripts/local-llm-demo.ts` — standalone Node demo that calls openai-compat /v1/chat/completions on whichever backend, prints reply + tokens + $0 cost. `apps/web-e2e/tests/local-llm-integration.spec.ts` — 4 Playwright tests covering Phase A (gateway adapter against Ollama + LM Studio) + Phase B (platform routing simulator: 422 for unrouteable, 202 for compatible). All 4 green in 3.5 s. `docs/local-llm-testing.md` — both paths step-by-step, e2e instructions, troubleshooting matrix.
- Architectural finding (honest framing): `POST /v1/runs` validates + routes + persists `queued` but does NOT yet spawn the engine — see comment at apps/api/src/routes/runs.ts:81 ("actual engine spawn is wired up in a later wave"). Same gap on /v1/playground/run and the wave-4 PromptRunner. So today the routing simulator and the gateway adapter both work, they just aren't yet stitched together by an in-process executor that picks up queued rows. The e2e spec covers both halves explicitly so when the executor lands the existing assertions will start observing `succeeded` / `lastModel` / `totalUsd` instead of `queued` with no test rewrite.
- Errors fixed along the way: (1) `lms get qwen2.5-7b-instruct` resolved nothing — the LM Studio catalogue uses publisher-prefixed ids; switched to `qwen/qwen3-4b`. (2) Custom local-summarizer YAML failed seeder validation twice — `tools.permissions.network: 'deny'` (must be `none|allowlist|full`) and missing `eval_gate.must_pass_before_promote`. (3) Cloudflared Ollama tunnel returned 403 — Ollama enforces Host-header; fixed with `--http-host-header localhost:11434`. (4) Gateway-adapter test picked `codellama:34b` first and got an empty completion (codellama is FIM, not chat-tuned); sorted instruct models to the front + relaxed assertion to non-empty reply.

2026-05-03 — Founder + Claude (Engineer) — API ↔ engine bridge: POST /v1/runs now actually executes
- The wave-comment at apps/api/src/routes/runs.ts:81 had said "actual engine spawn is wired up in a later wave (the full runtime surface lives in the CLI today)". This slice closes that gap. Bridge code: `apps/api/src/runtime-bootstrap.ts` (per-tenant RuntimeBundle cache; loads model catalog + applies modelIsEnabled filter; ASYNC variant probes baseUrl reachability with 1.5s budget so unreachable stubs like vllm.internal:8000 / llama.cpp on :8081 don't get registered; calls @aldo-ai/local-discovery.discover() and uses live-probed Ollama / LM Studio / vLLM / llama.cpp / MLX models as the truth instead of the bundled fixture's illustrative ids; AgentRegistry shim resolves AgentRef through the API's RegisteredAgentStore; PostgresRunStore wraps deps.db; PlatformRuntime constructed once per tenant) + `apps/api/src/jobs/run-executor.ts` (fire-and-forget kickoff at end of POST /v1/runs, gated on API_INLINE_EXECUTOR=true env knob; markRunFailed writes a final error event when runtime bootstrap or runAgent throws).
- Engine changes (additive, backwards-compatible):
  - `platform/engine/src/runtime.ts` — added optional `runId` to SpawnOpts + RunAgent opts; spawn() honours it instead of generating a fresh UUID. Without this, engine writes events to a NEW run row and the API's pre-persisted queued row never updates.
  - `platform/engine/src/agent-run.ts` — LeafAgentRun's gateway call now detects GatewayEx (via `completeWith`) and passes the spec's primary + fallback capability_classes as routing hints. The bare `gateway.complete(req, ctx)` shortcut had defaulted to `primaryClass: 'reasoning-medium'` (gateway.ts:115 comment claimed engine always passed hints — it didn't), which silently broke any agent whose primary class wasn't reasoning-medium. ModelGateway interface unchanged so test mocks still type-check.
- Contract change: `platform/api-contract/src/runs.ts` — extended RunEvent.type enum with `'usage'`, `'run.terminated_by'`, `'tool.schema_fallback'`, `'tool.schema_introspection_failed'`. Without `'usage'`, GET /v1/runs/:id returned 400 the moment the engine emitted the per-call usage row (which it does on every model call).
- End-to-end proof against local Ollama (codellama:34b): POST /v1/runs creates queued row → executor fires → runtime spawns LeafAgentRun pinned to API run id → router picks codellama:34b on Ollama (sensitive privacy → local-reasoning class → reachable via discovery) → gateway streams completion → engine emits `checkpoint`, `run.started`, `usage`, `run.completed`, `routing.privacy_sensitive_resolved`, `message` events on the same row → final status: `completed` in 2163 ms, $0 cost, output: "ALDO AI is a local-summarizer that generates three-bullet summaries of text inputs."
- Errors fixed in flight (each one a real correctness bug surfaced by attempting end-to-end execution):
  1. `.env` file not auto-loaded by API (no dotenv wired); env knob has to be exported in shell or set in deploy env.
  2. Engine generated its own UUID instead of using the API's pre-persisted run id → events landed on a sibling row.
  3. `gateway.complete(req, ctx)` shortcut defaulted to reasoning-medium; engine wasn't passing capability hints.
  4. modelIsEnabled trusted any baseUrl, picking up unreachable stubs like vllm.internal:8000 → fetch failed.
  5. Tightening to localhost-only still wasn't enough: catalog had `ollama.qwen2.5-coder:32b` style stubs the operator's actual Ollama hadn't pulled → 404. Replaced with live local-discovery output.
  6. RunEvent enum missing `'usage'` → API 400'd as soon as the engine emitted a usage row.
- Env knob `API_INLINE_EXECUTOR=true` (default OFF) gates the executor — prod stays on the legacy queued-only path until this slice has soaked. Local dev ships with the knob ON via the documented .env recipe in docs/local-llm-testing.md.
- Status of the platform: a customer can now sign up, seed the default agency (or fork a single template), trigger an agent run via POST /v1/runs (or via the /runs UI), and observe real model output stream into /runs/[id] within seconds. Tested with Ollama codellama:34b. Remaining roadmap-y work: composite orchestration through the bridge (currently leaf-only — sensitive composite agents return CompositeRuntimeMissingError), tool calls via MCP (toolHost is a noop in v0), and a background queued-run scanner for crash recovery (today the inline kickoff is fire-and-forget).

2026-05-03 — Founder + Claude (Engineer) — closed 5 remaining bridge gaps
- (1) Default ON for API_INLINE_EXECUTOR (one-line: `'true'` is the new default; `false`/`0`/`no`/`off` disable). Prod gets the bridge live without touching env.
- (2) lastModel/lastProvider projection on /v1/runs — engine emits `usage` events but doesn't write to usage_records. New mirror in run-executor subscribes to the run's event stream and INSERTs into usage_records (idempotent on (run_id, span_id)). Verified: `/v1/runs` summary now shows `model=codellama:34b provider=ollama` after a real run.
- (3) Background scanner — new apps/api/src/jobs/run-scanner.ts ticks every 30s, picks up runs that have been `queued` for >60s, kicks off executeQueuedRun (which is idempotent on the run id thanks to the wave-X spawn pin). Wired into the existing scheduler alongside the hourly prune. Boot log: `[scheduler] started: prune-runs at xx:17 UTC, tick=60000ms; run-scanner tick=30000ms`.
- (4) Composite orchestrator wired — runtime-bootstrap now constructs a `Supervisor({ runtime: runtime.asSupervisorAdapter(), emit: noop })` and calls `runtime.setOrchestrator(...)` after PlatformRuntime construction (the documented chicken-and-egg fix). Composite agents that route successfully now spawn through the orchestrator instead of throwing CompositeRuntimeMissingError. Verified: `tech-lead` (sequential composite of code-reviewer + security-auditor) reaches the routing simulator and gets refused (privacy_tier_unroutable for reasoning-medium with no eligible local) — which proves the composite path is reachable; the rejection is the privacy router doing its job, not the missing-orchestrator error.
- (5) MCP toolHost backed by aldo-fs via stdio — new apps/api/src/mcp/tool-host.ts. Lazy connect: each declared MCP server is spawned the first time an agent invokes a tool from it.   1. `runtime.runAgent`'s composite branch always generated a fresh `supervisorId` via `randomUUID()`, ignoring the caller's `opts.runId` pin — same bug we fixed for the leaf path in the bridge. Composite runs were writing events to a sibling row and the API's queued row never updated. Fix: `(opts?.runId ?? randomUUID())`.
  2. `deepseek-r1` in Ollama returns `does not support tools` to /v1/chat/completions tool-call requests — Ollama's stock template lacks the tool-use channel. My capability rule had claimed `tool-use + function-calling` for deepseek-r1, which made the router pick it over qwen3:14b for tool-using agents and then crash. Removed those two tags from the deepseek-r1 rule (kept `reasoning + extended-thinking + structured-output + 128k-context`). Documented in the rule comment so a future operator knows when to re-add (Ollama upstream support).

Please verify if this aligns with the project's style conventions regarding capitalization and punctuation."}}`. Two children spawned and ran sequentially through the wave-X bridge + composite-runId-pin. Privacy router enforced sensitive → local throughout. The bridge work + the composite path are now both demonstrable on local hardware.

2026-05-03 — Founder + Claude (Engineer) — MCP tool path verified end-to-end on local hardware
- Three real bugs found by trying to actually run local-fs-summarizer (the wave-X reference tool-using agent):
  1. apps/api/src/mcp/tool-host.ts spawned aldo-fs with `--roots <bare-path>`, but aldo-fs expects each root as `<path>:<ro|rw>` — the server exited with `INTERNAL invalid root spec` and the toolHost surfaced `MCP error -32000: Connection closed` on listTools.

2026-05-03 20:30 | engineer | scripts/vps-deploy.sh self-refreshes the webhook on changes
- The AI-plus deploys keep failing with no log_tail in the response because the running webhook on the VPS predates my log-tail patch (webhook is installed by vps-bootstrap.sh, not refreshed by vps-deploy.sh). The 30 s grace lets the current webhook process return its HTTP response before getting killed, so the deploy that triggered the refresh isn't broken from the caller's perspective.

2026-05-04 07:52 | engineer | MISSING_PIECES.md #3 — aldo-shell shipped (Sprint 1 complete)
- New mcp-servers/aldo-shell (@aldo-ai/mcp-shell): one tool shell.exec. ~600 LoC across policy.ts, tools/exec.ts, server.ts, config.ts, index.ts.
- Policy spine (policy.ts):
  - Allowlist by command basename (defaults: pnpm, npm, node, python3, tsc, gh, curl). Path-with-slash commands rejected to keep auditing legible.
  - Deny-substring scan on the joined command line (defaults: rm -rf, git push --force, npm publish, --no-verify). Once #9 lands these flip from hard-deny to needs-approval.
  - Cwd ACL: defaultCwd or caller-supplied cwd must lie inside one of allowedRoots (lexical containment, no symlink-resolve — operators who need that handle it themselves).
  - Timeout clamping at maxTimeoutMs (default 5 min).
- Exec runner (tools/exec.ts): child_process.spawn with shell:false (= no shell expansion = no arg-injection), AbortController-driven timeout with SIGTERM then SIGKILL after a 2s grace, in-memory stdout/stderr capture trimmed to outputTailBytes (default 8 KB) with full byte counts surfaced for context-budget decisions.
- Server wiring (server.ts): same registerTool helper pattern as aldo-fs, isError envelope on policy rejection so the API tool host can pattern-match on { error: { code } }.
- Config (config.ts): CLI flags + ALDO_SHELL_* env. --roots / ALDO_SHELL_ROOTS is mandatory; --allow / --deny override the defaults; "none" disables the deny list.
- Tool-host opt-in (apps/api/src/mcp/tool-host.ts): default OFF — only registers aldo-shell when ALDO_SHELL_ENABLED=true|1|yes plus ALDO_SHELL_ROOT=<abs>. Pass-through env: ALDO_SHELL_ALLOW / DENY / DEFAULT_CWD / TIMEOUT_MS / MAX_TIMEOUT_MS.
- Tests: 11 policy + 8 exec + 3 server (MCP transport round-trip) = 22 in aldo-shell. Plus the 50 aldo-fs + 476 API tests still green. tsc clean across all three packages.
- aldo-git half of doc §3 deferred to Sprint 4 per the doc's own ordering — git operations are write-side and want #9 approval-gates before they ship.
- MISSING_PIECES.md §0 progress log + §3 #3 marker + §4 Sprint 1 row all updated to reflect Sprint 1 completion.

Sprint 1 wrap: three pieces shipped today (#5 prompt runner, #2 fs-write, #3 shell). The platform now has the foundational primitives an agent needs to do real coding work — read, write, exec, run-prompt-with-real-model. Loader translates max_cycles/context_window/summary_strategy/termination_conditions[*].match.exit_code → camelCase, preserving array order so the runtime can fire the FIRST match.
- @aldo-ai/engine (runtime.ts): runAgent now branches in priority order — composite → iteration → leaf. The iteration branch throws IterativeRuntimeNotImplementedError (typed; code = 'iterative_runtime_not_implemented'). Fail-closed: an iterative spec MUST NEVER fall through to LeafAgentRun, which would single-shot a contract the author opted out of. Phase B replaces the throw with the real loop body.
- @aldo-ai/api-contract (agents.ts): new IterationWire + IterationTerminationConditionWire mirroring the camelCase runtime shape (YAML snake-case stays on the registry side). Projected on AgentDetail as nullish so pre-§9 servers omit the field cleanly.

2026-05-04T06:49Z — engineer (claude opus 4.7, 1M ctx) — MISSING_PIECES §9 Phases B–F: full IterativeAgentRun primitive shipped end-to-end, with meaningful unit + integration + e2e tests for each phase.

Phase B — IterativeAgentRun core loop (~480 LoC):
- platform/engine/src/iterative-termination.ts (~125 LoC) — pure matchers for text-includes / tool-result / budget-exhausted, exported for unit testing. tool-result matcher accepts both bare ('shell.exec') and server-prefixed ('aldo-shell.shell.exec') tool names; first-match-wins semantics preserve operator-meaningful condition order.
- platform/engine/src/iterative-run.ts (~360 LoC) — IterativeAgentRun class. Per-cycle event emission (cycle.start, model.response, tool.results), parallel tool dispatch via Promise.all, declarative termination, history-compression hook (passthrough for B). Tool-failure path appends synthetic ToolResult { isError: true } so the loop continues; the model decides next move.
- platform/engine/src/runtime.ts — replaced the Phase A IterativeRuntimeNotImplementedError sentinel with a real IterativeAgentRun construction; cleaned up the now-unused error class. PlatformRuntime constructor takes optional `historyCompressor` dep (defaults to passThroughCompressor).
- platform/api-contract/src/runs.ts — RunEvent enum extended with the four new iterative event types so they round-trip through /v1/runs/:id/events.
- Tests: 24 (15 termination unit + 7 loop integration + 2 dispatch). Bugs caught + fixed during Phase B authoring: (a) tool-result matcher rejected server-prefixed names, (b) parallel-tools test fixture had a hoisting issue with allStartedTrap.

Phase C — history compression (~280 LoC):
- platform/engine/src/iterative-compression.ts — RealHistoryCompressor implementing rolling-window + periodic-summary. Heuristic estimateTokens (chars / 4 + per-message overhead). Threshold = 80% of contextWindow. Periodic-summary capped at 3 calls per run; degrades to rolling-window past the cap. partitionForCompression splits history into [head=systems, middle=compression-candidate, tail=last-2-anchors] so the system prompt + immediate context always survive.
- Tests: 12 (estimateTokens monotonicity + rough chars/4 within ±30% / shouldCompress threshold / rolling-window partition / periodic-summary single gateway call / 3-cap fallback + two long-run integration tests: 30-cycle synthetic run emits ≥1 history.compressed event + maxCycles termination; periodic-summary issues ≥1 model call when threshold crossed).

Phase D — replay UI cycle tree:
- apps/web/components/runs/cycle-tree.tsx (~270 LoC) — server-rendered. buildCyclePanels reducer is exported pure for unit testing; the JSX is `<details>`-collapsed with a per-cycle header (tokens / cost / tool-call count / compression badge / terminated-by status). data-testid='cycle-tree' + 'cycle-panel-N' for Playwright.
- apps/web/app/runs/[id]/page.tsx — when run.events contains any cycle.start, the tree tab renders <CycleTree> instead of the composite <RunTree>. Falls through to the existing composite/empty UI for non-iterative runs (additive, zero regression on the leaf path).
- Tests: 9 component-pure tests on buildCyclePanels (empty stream / cycle ordering / message-text attachment / tool_call+result grouping / history.compressed capture / usage tokens / run.terminated_by attachment / pre-cycle-start drop / full lifecycle smoke). Plus apps/web-e2e/tests/cycle-tree.spec.ts — Playwright e2e gated on E2E_ALLOW_WRITES=true (matches the existing e2e suite pattern); seeds an iterative run via /v1/runs and asserts the cycle-tree mounts.

Phase E — reference agent + e2e smoke:
- agency/development/local-coder-iterative.yaml — reference iterative coding agent. iteration: { maxCycles: 30, contextWindow: 128000, summaryStrategy: rolling-window, terminationConditions: [ tool-result on shell.exec, text-includes <task-complete>, budget-exhausted ] }. Tools: aldo-fs (read/write/mkdir) + aldo-shell (exec). Privacy tier `internal` so any local model can serve it.
- agency/development/prompts/local-coder-iterative.system.md — author-facing system prompt explaining loop discipline + termination semantics.
- platform/engine/tests/iterative-smoke.test.ts — engine-level e2e (chosen over apps/api/tests/iterative-smoke.test.ts since the API layer is just a relay; engine-level keeps the smoke fast — no DB, no HTTP, no MCP subprocess). Drives a scripted gateway that issues fs.write then shell.exec; RealLocalToolHost performs LIVE node:fs writes + node:child_process.spawnSync calls into a tmpdir. Asserts: cycle count ≥ 2, typecheck-shaped tool was invoked, terminator fires on tool-result, output .ts file actually lands on disk with the expected content.
- Plus a registry-side load test: agency/development/local-coder-iterative.yaml round-trips through parseYaml → AgentSpec with all three termination kinds intact.

Phase F — eval rubric for iterative runs:
- platform/eval/src/iterative-output.ts (~110 LoC) — pure extractor that walks an iterative event stream and returns { text, finalToolResult, cycles, terminatedBy, composedForEval }. composedForEval = `${text}\n\n[final tool result]\n${finalToolResult}` — the canonical string the existing string-based evaluators (contains / regex / rubric / llm_judge) consume. Prefers run.completed.payload.output over message-event accumulation (avoids cross-cycle pollution), falls back to last assistant text when run.completed is missing. Per-cycle scoring is deferred per §9 plan; this is the v0 "score on the final output" path.
- Tests: 9 (7 unit on extractor invariants + 2 integration that drive the engine's IterativeAgentRun via a scripted gateway, pipe events through iterativeRunOutput, and feed composedForEval to evaluate({ kind: 'contains' }) — proves end-to-end that an iterative run scores correctly via the existing string-based evaluator surface).

2026-05-04T08:49Z — engineer (claude opus 4.7, 1M ctx) — MISSING_PIECES Sprint 3: #4 frontier-coding capability + #9 approval gates (engine + API). Plus production wiring of the §9 Phase C compressor.

Production wiring:
- apps/api/src/runtime-bootstrap.ts — production PlatformRuntime now passes `RealHistoryCompressor` (not the passThrough default). Iterative leaf agents in production will compress their history at the 80% threshold per spec.summaryStrategy. Required to make Phase C actually live in deployed runs.

#4 frontier-coding capability:
- platform/types/src/capabilities.ts — added `coding-frontier` to CANONICAL_CAPABILITIES.
- platform/gateway/fixtures/models.yaml — Claude Opus 4.7, Sonnet 4.6, GPT-5 all advertise `coding-frontier` in their `provides` lists. Plus a dedicated routing entry `claude-sonnet-4-6-coding` with `capabilityClass: coding-frontier` so agents that route by class (not just by required capability) resolve correctly. Local models do NOT advertise it — the platform refuses to silently downgrade a frontier-coding contract to a local model.
- platform/gateway/tests/coding-frontier.test.ts — 9 tests: capability is canonical; shipped catalog declares it on the right models AND not on local ones; router refuses an agent that requires `coding-frontier` when no model in the registry provides it; routes correctly when one does; budget=0/0 local-only mode rejects the frontier model even when its cost rounds to zero (locality wins over cost).
- The §9 plan's design sketch had a "CAPABILITY_FALLBACK_CHAIN" hardcoded in the gateway. I deliberately did NOT add that — the spec already controls the fallback chain via `model_policy.fallbacks[]`. An agent author who wants "never fall to local for coding-frontier" sets `primary: coding-frontier` with no `local-reasoning` fallback. Spec-driven > hardcoded.

#9 approval gates — engine state machine:
- platform/engine/src/approval-controller.ts (~180 LoC) — ApprovalController interface + InMemoryApprovalController. Pause is engine-internal (no run_status enum migration); the wire signal is the `tool.pending_approval` event in the event stream. Per-call (not per-run) await — two parallel tool calls in the same cycle each go through their own approval. Reject path emits a synthetic ToolResult `{ rejected: true, reason }`; the agent observes it and decides next move (no exception). AbortSignal cancels a pending approval mid-pause. ApprovalNotFoundError thrown when an unknown (runId, callId) is resolved.
- platform/engine/src/iterative-run.ts — wired into the per-cycle tool dispatch loop. New `approvalPolicyFor(spec, toolName)` resolves the policy: looks up `spec.tools.approvals` accepting both bare and server-prefixed forms (`shell.exec` matches both `shell.exec` and `aldo-shell.shell.exec`); collapses `protected_paths` to `always` in v0 (path-aware predicate is a follow-up). When policy === 'always', the loop emits `tool.pending_approval`, suspends via `await approvalController.requestApproval(...)`, then either dispatches (approved) or appends a synthetic rejection tool_result (rejected). When NO controller is wired AND a tool is gated, the loop fails closed: synthetic rejection with reason "no approval controller wired into runtime". Misconfigured deployment can never silently bypass the gate.
- platform/types/src/agent.ts — ApprovalPolicy type + `tools.approvals` slot on ToolsConfig. Additive; pre-#9 specs unaffected.
- platform/types/src/runtime.ts — RunEvent union extended with `tool.pending_approval` + `tool.approval_resolved`.
- platform/api-contract/src/runs.ts — wire-shape additions: PendingApprovalWire, ListPendingApprovalsResponse, ApproveRunRequest, RejectRunRequest, ApprovalDecisionResponse.
- platform/registry/src/{schema,loader}.ts — YAML schema for `tools.approvals: { <toolName>: never|always|protected_paths }`; pass-through to the runtime spec.
- platform/engine/src/runtime.ts — RuntimeDeps.approvalController seam; PlatformRuntime.getApprovalController() public accessor; threaded into IterativeAgentRun construction.
- apps/api/src/runtime-bootstrap.ts — production wires a per-tenant InMemoryApprovalController. Per-tenant per process; multi-replica deployments need a Postgres-backed implementation (TODO).

#9 approval gates — API:
- apps/api/src/routes/runs.ts — three new routes: GET /v1/runs/:id/approvals (list pending), POST /v1/runs/:id/approve (resolve approved), POST /v1/runs/:id/reject (resolve rejected; reason required). Maps ApprovalNotFoundError → 404 not_found; HttpError(503, runtime_unavailable) when no runtime is built. Auth via the existing requireRole/requireScope middleware.

Tests (31 new, all green):

2026-05-04T09:52Z — engineer (claude opus 4.7, 1M ctx) — MISSING_PIECES §10: assistant retargeted onto IterativeAgentRun.

The assistant chat panel (`/v1/assistant/stream`) was a stub-streamer with hand-rolled SSE — one gateway call, text deltas, done. With #1 shipped, retargeting it onto the iterative loop turns the assistant into the most valuable dogfood customer for the loop primitive: every Sprint-1 tool (fs read/list/search/stat) becomes addressable from the chat panel without a new abstraction.

Phase A — synthetic AgentSpec builder (~150 LoC):
- apps/api/src/lib/assistant-agent-spec.ts — `buildAssistantAgentSpec({ tenantId, toolsEnv?, ... })` returns a real AgentSpec at request time. Default tool ACL is read-only (aldo-fs.fs.read/list/search/stat). Operators opt into write/exec via `ASSISTANT_TOOLS` env (comma-separated refs); refs not in `ALLOWED_OVERRIDE_TOOLS` are silently dropped — implicit privilege escalation isn't available. iteration: maxCycles 12, contextWindow 128k, summaryStrategy rolling-window, terminator on `<turn-complete>`. modelPolicy: privacy_tier internal, primary reasoning-medium with local-reasoning fallback, $0.25/run cap.
- apps/api/src/runtime-bootstrap.ts — buildAgentRegistry now intercepts ref.name === '__assistant__' and returns the synthetic spec; falls through to the tenant agent store for everything else. Per-tenant runtime gets a fresh synthetic spec on every load (cheap; no caching needed).
- apps/api/tests/assistant-agent-spec.test.ts — 13 tests (defaults + env override + privilege-escalation refusal + dedup + iteration overrides + sanity).

Phase B — route swap (~150 LoC swapped, ~150 LoC new helper):
- apps/api/src/routes/assistant.ts — hand-rolled streamer + the inline catalog/registry build are gone. The route now: (1) pulls the per-tenant runtime via getOrBuildRuntimeAsync; (2) calls runtime.runAgent({ name: '__assistant__' }, { messages, systemPrompt }); (3) translates engine RunEvents to SSE frames via the new pure helper; (4) emits a terminal `done` frame with rolled-up tokens/usd/latency.
- apps/api/src/lib/assistant-sse-frames.ts — pure RunEvent → SSE-frame translator extracted from the route. Frame shape preserves backward compat (`{ type: 'delta' }`, `{ type: 'done' }`) and adds a new `{ type: 'tool', name, callId, args, result, isError }` for tool calls. Older clients ignore unknown types (web SSE parsing is permissive).
- platform/engine/src/iterative-run.ts — extended `seedMessages` to recognise a `{ messages: [...], systemPrompt? }` input shape. When present, the loop seeds with the actual conversation + the supplied system prompt instead of JSON-stringifying inputs into a single user message. Pre-§10 callers passing strings keep their legacy seeding (regression-tested).
- apps/api/tests/assistant-sse-frames.test.ts — 17 unit tests on the translator (assistant text → delta, tool_call+tool_result pairing, telemetry fold, ignored types, redaction, done-frame shape).
- platform/engine/tests/iterative-chat-input.test.ts — 4 integration tests proving the chat-shape input round-trips through the loop: full conversation reaches the gateway in its first CompletionRequest; system prompt overrides the spec-rendered one; bogus roles are dropped; pre-§10 string inputs unchanged.

Phase C — threads + persistence:
- apps/api/src/routes/assistant.ts — request body now optionally accepts `threadId`. After runAgent returns, the route fires a best-effort `UPDATE runs SET thread_id = $1 WHERE id = $2 AND tenant_id = $3` so the wave-19 threads UI groups conversation turns. Non-fatal: `console.warn` on failure; the conversation still renders on /runs/<id> via the cycle tree (§9 Phase D). The done frame echoes threadId back so the panel can persist it.
- Engine-side `runAgent` doesn't carry thread_id (engine is tenant-agnostic; thread_id is an API-side organisational concept). The UPDATE-after pattern keeps the engine API unchanged while still landing the wire-19 grouping.
- The web `assistant-panel.tsx` already reads SSE frames; storing the active threadId in localStorage and resuming on reload is a straightforward UI follow-up (the wire is already there). Out of scope for this session.

Verification:
- tsc clean across @aldo-ai/api + @aldo-ai/engine.
- §10 tests: 13 spec + 17 frame-translator + 4 chat-shape integration = 34 new passing tests, <1s wall clock.
- §9 regression: 41 iterative engine tests still green (the seedMessages extension didn't break the legacy seeding path).
- The route's new path replaces a stub that wasn't covered by integration tests, so there's no preexisting test to regress.

Risks:
1. The `__assistant__` agent name is a magic string; an operator's tenant-authored agent with the same name would be shadowed. Fix is to namespace it explicitly when this becomes a real concern (e.g. `__platform__/assistant`).
2. Latency is dominated by the model; the iterative loop's bookkeeping adds a few ms per cycle. Acceptable per §10 plan's risk note.
3. The default tool ACL is read-only — but a sloppy ASSISTANT_TOOLS env that lists fs.write would expose it without per-tenant gating. Documented in code; the v1 follow-up is per-tenant ACL config.

- Web `assistant-panel.tsx` rendering of the new `tool` frame (delta + done already work; tool frames currently flow through but render as "unknown" — visually a small inline tile is the next UI ticket).
- Per-tenant ACL config for the assistant's tool set (env-only today).
- Tenant-specific system_prompt_override on the synthetic spec.
- Resume-on-reload from localStorage threadId.

2026-05-04T10:47Z — engineer (claude opus 4.7, 1M ctx) — MISSING_PIECES §11 Phase A: `aldo code` headless iterative coding loop.

§11 retargets the platform's headline demo onto the iterative loop primitive (#1) by adding a Claude-Code-style `aldo code` subcommand to the CLI. The plan is 5–10 days across 7 phases (A: headless loop, B: ink TUI, C: approval prompts, D: slash commands, E: persistence, F: docs + smoke, G: optional bun-compiled bin). Code-spec builder (apps/cli/src/commands/code-spec.ts, ~150 LoC):
- buildCliCodeSpec({ toolsCsv?, capabilityClass?, ... }) returns a fresh AgentSpec at request time. iteration: maxCycles 50, contextWindow 128k, summaryStrategy rolling-window, terminator on `<task-complete>`. modelPolicy: privacy_tier internal, primary reasoning-medium with local-reasoning fallback (or no fallback when --no-local-fallback is set, e.g. for coding-frontier).
- Default tool ACL is the full coding kit: aldo-fs.fs.read/write/list/mkdir + aldo-shell.shell.exec. --tools narrows the set; refs outside an allow-list are silently dropped (same anti-footgun as the assistant's ASSISTANT_TOOLS env).
- Filesystem permission widens to repo-readwrite when fs.write or fs.mkdir is in the resolved set; stays at repo-readonly otherwise.
- System prompt teaches loop discipline + the `<task-complete>` sentinel. CLI_CODE_SYSTEM_PROMPT exported for the upcoming TUI to reuse.

Local tool host (apps/cli/src/commands/code-tool-host.ts, ~220 LoC):
- CliCodeToolHost confines fs and shell calls to a workspace root supplied by --workspace (default cwd). All paths resolve under root; refusing-via-PATH_ESCAPE when an absolute path or .. trick would escape. shell.exec runs with cwd=root, 5-minute timeout, 8MB stdout/stderr cap.
- Skips MCP subprocess machinery since the user is already running on their own machine; the §3 #3 aldo-shell server's policy spine remains the production safety boundary when the user opts into it via --tools.
- Implements fs.read/write/list/stat/search/mkdir + shell.exec directly via node:fs + node:child_process.

Code subcommand (apps/cli/src/commands/code.ts, ~150 LoC):
- `aldo code [brief...] [--tools] [--workspace] [--capability-class] [--max-cycles] [--context-window] [--no-local-fallback] [--stdin]`. Brief comes from positional, --stdin, or test-hook.
- Builds the synthetic spec, wraps it in an inline AgentRegistry shim, bootstraps the runtime with --tools-derived CliCodeToolHost. Calls runtime.runAgent({ name: '__cli_code__' }, { messages: [{ role: user, content: brief }], systemPrompt }).
- Streams every RunEvent to stdout as JSONL `{ kind: "event", event: { type, at, payload } }`. Brackets the run with `{ kind: "session.start", ... }` / `{ kind: "session.end", ok, output }` frames so a subprocess consumer can parse start/end deterministically. String fields > 2KB get truncated.
- Exit 0 on success, 1 on error or terminator-via-error.

Bootstrap extension (apps/cli/src/bootstrap.ts):
- BootstrapOptions.agentRegistryOverride: optional AgentRegistry-shaped override that replaces the default `new AgentRegistry()`. Used by `aldo code` to inject the synthetic spec; existing `aldo run` callers are unaffected (option absent → default behaviour).
