- apps/cli/tests/code-spec.test.ts — 14 unit tests covering defaults, --tools narrowing + dedup + privilege-escalation refusal, fs.write widening filesystem permission, capability-class override, refuseLocalFallback, sanity (privacy tier, budget cap).
- apps/cli/tests/code-command.test.ts — 3 integration tests against runCode with a stub gateway: scripted cycle 1 (fs.write hello.ts) → cycle 2 (shell.exec printf "tsc OK") → cycle 3 (text <task-complete>); asserts exit 0, JSONL frames, real file landing on disk, shell.exec dispatched, terminator reason text-includes; missing-brief returns exit 1; --tools narrowing fails-closed when the agent attempts an unallowed tool.

2026-05-04T11:01Z — engineer (claude opus 4.7, 1M ctx) — MISSING_PIECES §11 Phase B: ink TUI shell for `aldo code`.

State reducer (apps/cli/src/commands/code/state.ts, ~250 LoC):

2026-05-04T11:20Z — engineer (claude opus 4.7, 1M ctx) — MISSING_PIECES §11 Phase C: approval prompts in the `aldo code` TUI.

Phase C closes the safety loop in the TUI. Tool calls whose spec marks them `tools.approvals: always` (the same #9 mechanism the run-detail page surfaces in the web banner) suspend the iterative loop in-process; the App now renders a modal-style dialog and routes a/r/v keybinds to the controller.

Bootstrap extension (apps/cli/src/bootstrap.ts):
- BootstrapOptions.approvalController: optional ApprovalController. Wired into PlatformRuntime when supplied. Headless `aldo code` leaves it undefined → gated tools fail closed via the engine's synthetic rejection (matches every other unattended caller). The TUI builds a fresh InMemoryApprovalController per session and threads it both into the runtime AND into the App's keybind handler.

State reducer extension (commands/code/state.ts):
- The awaiting-approval phase now carries the full payload — { runId, callId, tool, args, reason } — so the dialog has everything it needs for rendering AND so the App can call `controller.resolve(runId, callId, ...)` correctly. The runId is required (not optional) because resolve() keys on the (runId, callId) tuple.
- Reducer drops malformed events (missing runId, callId, OR tool); 24 reducer tests now cover the richer payload + the malformed-event path.

ApprovalDialog component (~80 LoC):
- Three sub-states: choose / viewing / rejecting. Choose lands by default and shows `[a]pprove · [r]eject · [v]iew-full-args`. Viewing expands the args JSON multi-line. Rejecting focuses an inline reason input with Enter-to-confirm / Esc-to-cancel.
- Pure renderer — sub-state owned by the App and reset on each new pending callId so consecutive approvals don't reuse a half-typed reject draft.
- 7 ink-testing-library tests cover all three sub-states + the agent-reason / no-reason rendering / args truncation / multi-line expansion.

App keybind wiring (commands/code/app.tsx):
- useInput with `isActive: phase === 'awaiting-approval'` so the dialog's keys never collide with the regular Input's typing.
- a/A → approve and resolve via `controller.resolve(runId, callId, { kind: 'approved' })`. The next engine event (tool_result for the dispatched call) flips the phase back to running.
- r/R → enter rejecting sub-state. Enter sends `controller.resolve(... { kind: 'rejected', reason })`; Esc returns to choose.
- v/V → toggle viewing sub-state for full args.
- Backspace + printable chars edit the reject reason draft.

2026-05-04T11:54Z — engineer (claude opus 4.7, 1M ctx) — MISSING_PIECES §11 Phase D: slash commands + transcript export.

Phase D adds the small but high-leverage in-session controls every Claude-Code-style TUI ships: /help, /clear, /save <path>, /exit, plus read-only /model and /tools. Mid-session model + tool swap is deferred (would require a fresh runtime + spec rebuild and history transfer); read-only views are the right v0 affordance.

Slash command parser + transcript renderer (commands/code/slash-commands.ts, ~140 LoC):
- parseSlashCommand(text): SlashCommand | null. Returns null when text doesn't start with `/` so the App falls through to the regular user-input path. Discriminated union: help / clear / exit / save{path} / model / tools / unknown{raw}. Aliases supported (?  /reset /quit /q). Case-insensitive command name. /save without a path returns 'unknown' so the App can show a clear error.
- HELP_TEXT — exported as data so the help dispatch is one dispatch into a system-info action; tests assert every command + keybind is mentioned.
- renderTranscriptMarkdown(entries): pure markdown emitter. ## you / ## aldo / ### tool · <name> · ok|error|pending / ### system. JSON-fenced args + result.

State extension (commands/code/state.ts):
- New SystemEntry { kind: 'system', content }; new system-info action; reducer appends a SystemEntry without disturbing the running/idle/etc. phase. Pre-Phase D entries unchanged.

Conversation rendering: ※ system header + dim text for SystemEntry. Reducer's reset-conversation action (already shipping in Phase B) doubles as /clear.

App intercept (commands/code/app.tsx):
- startTurn parses slash commands BEFORE dispatching user-input. Each command branches: /help → system-info(HELP_TEXT); /clear → reset-conversation; /exit → abort + ink exit(); /save → renders transcript via stateRef.current.entries, calls onSave (injected by tui.ts) → confirms with system-info("transcript saved to ..."); /model and /tools → system-info displaying sessionInfo (capabilityClass / toolRefs); unknown → system-info hint.
- Used a stateRef so the /save handler can read the latest entries without making the callback rebuild on every state change (avoiding a stale-closure bug).

Side-effect bridges (commands/code/tui.ts):
- onSave(path, content): writes via mkdirSync(recursive) + writeFileSync, returning the resolved absolute path. Confines via cwd resolution but doesn't sandbox into the workspace root — operators saving a transcript to ~/notes is the common case.
- sessionInfo: capabilityClass + toolRefs + workspace + maxCycles surfaced to App for /model and /tools.

Tests: 78 §11 passing total (+17 Phase D). 13 parser cases (every command + aliases + missing-args + case-insensitivity + typos + non-slash falls through), HELP_TEXT shape assertion, 4 transcript-renderer cases (empty / full session / pending+error tool / streaming-vs-finished assistant / no-text placeholder), 2 reducer cases (system-info appends; preserves prior entries). tsc clean. Pre-existing CLI flake unchanged.

- Phase E — session persistence + --resume against the run store.
- Phase F — docs + smoke + bin polish.

2026-05-04T12:28Z — engineer (claude opus 4.7, 1M ctx) — MISSING_PIECES §11 Phase E: session persistence + --resume.

Phase E gives `aldo code --tui` cross-session memory. Each session is keyed by a UUID thread-id; the conversation Entry list is serialised to a JSON sidecar after every state change; `aldo code --tui --resume <thread-id>` rehydrates the App from the saved sidecar. Multi-day workflows (start Monday, resume Tuesday) preserve context.

Pragmatic v0 design — sidecar over a DB-rebuild path:
The §11 plan called for "write every turn into the platform's runs DB via the runtime's existing RunStore" and re-derive the UI state from RunEvents on resume. That's correct for replay (`/runs/<id>` cycle tree) but heavyweight for the chat-resume UX: re-running the reducer over a persisted event log on every session open is wasteful when the Entry list is the cached projection of those events. Phase E ships the sidecar as the UI's local memory; the DB still holds the engine RunEvents for replay (when DATABASE_URL is set, via the existing PostgresRunStore wiring), and a future improvement can also UPDATE runs.thread_id so /runs/<id> groups by thread alongside the sidecar.

Persistence module (commands/code/persistence.ts, ~210 LoC):
- saveSession({ threadId, workspace, entries, createdAt? }) writes ~/.aldo/code-sessions/<thread-id>.json (configurable via $ALDO_CODE_HOME or the test-only sessionsDir option). Atomic via tmp + rename so a crash mid-write can't corrupt a prior save. Preserves createdAt across re-saves; advances updatedAt every time.
- loadSession(threadId): returns SessionRecord or throws SessionNotFoundError / SessionCorruptError. Both error classes carry a typed `code` field for callers that want to branch on the failure mode.
- newThreadId(): UUID v4.
- listSessions(): newest-first by updatedAt; useful for a future `aldo code list` subcommand.
- sessionPath: anti-path-escape sanitiser; `[^a-zA-Z0-9_-]` chars become `_` so an adversarial `--resume "../../etc/passwd"` lands at `..___..___etc_passwd.json` inside the sessions dir.

State extension:
- New `hydrate-entries` action that REPLACES the entry list and resets phase to idle / lastError to null. Distinct from reset-conversation (which clears everything); hydrate seeds from a saved snapshot.

App wiring (commands/code/app.tsx):
- Two new optional props: `initialEntries` and `onPersist`.
- useEffect on first mount: if initialEntries is non-empty, dispatch hydrate-entries.
- useEffect on every state.entries change: call onPersist(state.entries) so the sidecar stays current. Skips the pre-hydration mount via a ref so we don't overwrite a saved session with an empty list.

TUI integration (commands/code/tui.ts):
- threadId = opts.resumeThreadId ?? newThreadId(). On --resume, loadSession; failures emit a clean error and exit 1. On a fresh session, prints both the threadId AND the resume command line so the user knows how to come back.
- onPersist callback writes the sidecar; failures emit a non-fatal warning (the in-memory conversation is untouched).
- Headless `aldo code` is unaffected.

2026-05-04T23:49Z — engineer (claude opus 4.7, 1M ctx) — aldo-git Phases B+C+D landed.

Phase B (write ops): git.add (rejects ".", "*", "**", "-"-prefixed, paths that escape repo root, paths that don't exist), git.checkout (refuses dirty tree without allowDirty; supports create + startPoint), git.commit (refuses protected-branch commits, refuses detached HEAD, schema-layer disallows --amend / --no-verify by simply not exposing them).

Phase C (remote ops): git.fetch / git.pull (--ff-only hard-coded — diverged history fails with a clean error rather than a merge commit) / git.push (force=no default; force=with-lease returns NEEDS_APPROVAL until #9 wires; plain --force is unreachable from the schema; rejects unknown remotes via assertRemoteAllowed).

2026-05-05T00:10Z — engineer (claude opus 4.7, 1M ctx) — §12.2 / #6 aldo-memory MCP (item 5.2 from the dry-run punch list).

The §13 Phase F post-mortem named aldo-memory as the long pole (3-5 days). v0 ships in this session. Backed by filesystem JSON, not Postgres — and that's the right call for unblocking the dry-run.

mcp-servers/aldo-memory/ (new package, @aldo-ai/mcp-memory):
- src/policy.ts — tenant allowlist, key shape (no .., /, \, NUL; 256B cap), retention as ISO 8601 duration, scope arity validation. fixedAgentName / fixedRunId optional pins for per-agent server spawning.
- src/store.ts — JSON files at <root>/<tenant>/<scope>/[<agentName>|<runId>/]<encoded-key>.json. Write-then-rename for atomicity. Scan honours prefix + limit, sorts newest-first by `at`. Delete is idempotent (returns deleted=false when absent).
- src/tools/{read,write,scan,delete}.ts — each tool 30-60 LoC, all four registered in src/server.ts.
- src/config.ts — CLI flags + env (ALDO_MEMORY_ROOT, ALDO_MEMORY_TENANTS required; ALDO_MEMORY_FIXED_AGENT, ALDO_MEMORY_FIXED_RUN, ALDO_MEMORY_MAX_KEY_BYTES, ALDO_MEMORY_MAX_VALUE_BYTES optional).
- src/index.ts — stdio entry.
- 3 test files: policy.test.ts (16 cases), store.test.ts (9), tools.test.ts (11). Total 36/36 green; covers cross-day continuity (a fresh policy reads prior writes), private+session partitioning, all four tools, and the §12.2 motivation directly.

2026-05-05T11:05Z — engineer (claude opus 4.7, 1M ctx) — §13 / item 5.5a live-mode harness + a discovered engine gap.

apps/api/tests/agency-dry-run/healthz-db.ts: extended runDryRun with mode 'live' and 'live:network'. Live mode (no network) wires real PlatformRuntime + real Supervisor + InMemoryRunStore + StubGateway + StubToolHost + MapBackedRegistry against the loaded agency YAMLs. The whole stack is the same one apps/api uses in production for composite runs (modulo gateway/tool stubbing).

What live mode v0 proved:
- Engine's runtime.runAgent() routes composite specs through the orchestrator branch.
- Supervisor.runComposite → SupervisorRuntimeAdapter.spawnChild → PlatformRuntime.spawn chain works against real agency-YAML specs with privacy cascade + run-store linkage honored.
- composite.{child_started, child_completed, usage_rollup} fire and roll up the stub gateway's per-leaf usage.
- 2 runs land in the store (supervisor + architect-as-leaf).

What live mode v0 surfaced (real engine finding):
- PlatformRuntime.spawn (runtime.ts:422) ALWAYS creates a LeafAgentRun regardless of whether the loaded spec carries a composite block.
- So when the architect (sequential[tech-lead, backend-engineer]) runs as a CHILD, its own composite is silently skipped.
- Whole tree should be 6+ runs deep; currently lands 2.
- The orchestrator's engine-integration.test.ts only exercised 1-level composite trees, which is why the gap wasn't observable.
- This is item 5.6: ~1-2 d engine fix. (1) detect composite in spawn() and dispatch through orchestrator, (2) make asSupervisorAdapter wait/collectUsage handle CompositeAgentRun returns too, (3) add 2-level composite test that fails without the fix.

Tests: 12/12 dry-run cases (was 8; +4 live mode), 541/541 apps/api total (was 537), tsc clean. Live-mode post-mortem at agency/dry-runs/2026-05-05-healthz-db-live.md. Full §11 update in 2026-05-04-healthz-db.md naming the gap as item 5.6 and walking through the proposed fix.

Honest call: the agency primitive ships in stub form + 1-level live form. Item 5.6 (engine spawn recursion) blocks the multi-level live dry-run; item 5.5b (live with real provider creds) blocks the real PR. After 5.6, 5.5b is straightforward. After 5.5b, the agency primitive ships against a real customer-shaped repo.

Found a real engine gap without spending a single dollar of inference. Exactly what §13 Phase F was designed to do.

2026-05-05T14:05Z — engineer (claude opus 4.7, 1M ctx) — §13 / item 5.6 engine spawn recursion landed; closes the gap 5.5a found.

platform/engine/src/runtime.ts:
- New private `spawnCompositeWrapper(ref, spec, inputs, opts)` helper that builds the supervisor wrapper run, records it on the run store, and dispatches to orchestrator.runComposite. Used by both runAgent (top-level composite roots, depth=0) and spawn's new composite branch (nested composites, depth=parent+1) so the recursion logic lives in exactly one place.
- spawn() now detects spec.composite !== undefined after loading the spec and routes through spawnCompositeWrapper before falling through to LeafAgentRun construction. This is the actual fix — pre-fix, spawn always built a leaf regardless of composite shape.
- Depth tracking added to runMeta. Every spawn (composite or leaf) computes its child's depth from the parent's runMeta entry. Decouples depth from SpawnOpts plumbing.
- CompositeAgentRun.collectUsage() shim added — returns [totalUsage] once the composite resolves, so the supervisor adapter treats composite child returns uniformly with leaf returns.
- asSupervisorAdapter() branches on this.composites.get(id) vs this.runs.get(id) and returns the right wait/collectUsage closure. Composite handles forward to the cached totalUsage; leaf handles do the existing per-run walk through runs.

platform/orchestrator/tests/engine-integration.test.ts:
- New test "recurses through nested composite specs (item 5.6 — full cascade)" that builds a 2-level composite (outer → middle → leaf-x + leaf-y) and asserts all 4 runs land in the store with correct parent/root linkage. Fails on the pre-fix engine.

apps/api/tests/agency-dry-run/healthz-db.test.ts:
- "expands the FULL composite cascade through every level" replaces the old "surfaces the engine gap" case. Asserts ≥6 runs in the store + all 5 expected child agents (architect, tech-lead, code-reviewer, security-auditor, backend-engineer) spawn.
- "emits one composite.usage_rollup per composite level" asserts exactly 3 rollups (principal + architect + tech-lead).

Live-mode dry-run output (re-rendered to agency/dry-runs/2026-05-05-healthz-db-live.md):
- ✅ composite completed
- 6 runs in store (was 2)
- 5 children spawn: architect, tech-lead, code-reviewer, security-auditor, backend-engineer
- 3 composite.usage_rollup events (one per composite level)

Verification:
- @aldo-ai/orchestrator: 53/53 tests (was 52, +1 2-level test).
- @aldo-ai/api: 542/542 (was 541, +1 from dry-run test rebalance).
- @aldo-ai/engine: pre-existing pglite-related flake in postgres-run-store.test.ts (event-order assertion); fails on stashed pre-change tree too. Not caused by this commit.
- All typechecks clean.

Net: the agency primitive ships in stub form AND in full multi-level live form. Item 5.5b (real provider creds + real MCP tool host) is the only remaining piece before a real PR landing on a real remote. ~1-2 days of wiring; the structure is the same as 5.5a, just with createGateway + createMcpToolHost in place of the stubs. After that: agency primitive ships against a customer-shaped repo.

Tangential conversation: discussed how the hosted ai.aldo.tech API would reach a user's local Ollama (firewall-blocked from the cloud). Two paths recommended: (A) Hybrid CLI — aldo binary runs locally for local-only agents, delegates cloud agents to hosted; (B) aldo bridge daemon — Bun-compiled cross-platform binary user installs, opens authenticated outbound tunnel. Cross-platform: macOS + Linux trivial; Windows needs EV cert (~$300-500/yr). Captured in auto-memory; not in MISSING_PIECES yet (separate distribution track).

2026-05-05T14:30Z — engineer (claude opus 4.7, 1M ctx) — §14 distribution & topology section drafted in MISSING_PIECES.md.

§14 captures the three orthogonal distribution / topology tracks that came up in conversation today: (A) local-model bridge — how hosted ai.aldo.tech reaches a user's local Ollama; (B) mobile + cross-device access — phone reaching a hosted run, laptop reaching a home `aldo` rig; (C) messaging channel fan-out — Telegram, email, Slack, etc. for approval gates and run notifications.

Key framing decisions captured in §14:
- The three tracks share three pieces of shared infra: outbound tunnel daemon (Bun-compiled, cross-platform), device-pairing flow (QR-code → token), event fan-out primitive. Building one earns most of the others cheaply; skipping one trades savings now for retro cost later.
- Recommended sequencing ranks Hybrid CLI (cheapest local-model story) + NotificationFanOut + Telegram/email first — they unlock unsupervised-agency-from-anywhere with ~5-6 days of total effort. PWA + Web Push + responsive UI follow as ~2 weeks. `aldo bridge` daemon + `aldo serve` cross-device tunnel are the larger product investments (~3-4 weeks combined, macOS+Linux first; Windows in v0.5 due to EV cert cost).
- Native iOS/Android apps deferred — web push is good enough for v0.
- WhatsApp / Viber / MS Teams / SMS deferred to per-customer-ask. Architecture is identical to Telegram; each is just another adapter behind NotificationFanOut.
- Two-way agency-as-chatbot (Telegram bot becomes the frontend, not just a notification channel) is called out as a separate initiative for after §14 lands.

Total spread: ~10-12 weeks for §14-A through §14-F sequentially by one engineer; most parallelisable.

§14 explicitly does NOT block any of the §13 dogfood smoke work — the agency primitive ships in three forms today (stub / live no-network / live:network), and §14 is what turns "works for us internally" into "works for a user in São Paulo on her phone."

Out-of-scope listed: federated multi-tenant bridge mesh, custom enterprise on-prem appliance (separate track from the existing self-hosted container path).

2026-05-05T18:15Z — engineer (claude opus 4.7, 1M ctx) — §13 dogfood smoke + harness fixes; §12.5 engagement-level budget cap shipped.

Item #1 — Live:network smoke against local Ollama (no frontier creds, $0 cost):
- Disposable worktree at /tmp/aldo-dryrun-1777996555 (git init + README seed).
- Env: ALDO_DRY_RUN_LIVE=1, ALDO_LOCAL_DISCOVERY=ollama, OLLAMA_BASE_URL=http://localhost:11434, ALDO_FS_RW_ROOT, ALDO_SHELL_ENABLED+_ROOT, ALDO_GIT_ENABLED+_ROOT, ALDO_MEMORY_ENABLED+_ROOT+_TENANTS.
- Local Ollama has deepseek-r1:32b, qwen3:14b, codellama:34b, gemma3n:latest — capability classes match agency YAML (`local-reasoning` fallback for principal/architect).

Three real smoke-harness gaps surfaced AND fixed:
1. **providerState cache poisoning between sibling tests.** The CI-default test pins `ALDO_LOCAL_DISCOVERY=none` to exercise the no-providers path; that empty `enabledModels` list was cached for the test process and any subsequent live:network smoke saw "no providers configured" even with Ollama running.
   FIX: `apps/api/src/runtime-bootstrap.ts` exports `resetProviderStateCacheForLiveDryRun()`. `runLiveNetworkMode` calls it before resolving so the operator's env always wins.
2. **`runStoreCount` was undefined in failure paths.** The `failure(...)` helper didn't populate `runStoreCount`; downstream `expect(runStoreCount).toBeGreaterThanOrEqual(1)` crashed with "actual value must be number or bigint, received undefined" instead of surfacing the real failure.
   FIX: `failure(...)` now sets `runStoreCount: 0` and a new `failureReason: string` field on `DryRunResult`. Test asserts via `result.failureReason !== undefined → throw`, surfacing the operator-facing reason.
3. **No programmatic failure surface.** Reasons were embedded only in the post-mortem markdown, forcing callers to grep prose for "no providers configured".
   FIX: `failureReason?: string` on `DryRunResult`; `tests/agency-dry-run/run-live-network.mjs` operator script prints it explicitly.

Real finding from item #1 (NOT yet fixed; recorded as next punch list): the live:network smoke wedges between bootstrap and runtime.runAgent — process at 0% CPU, 544 KB RSS, no Ollama model loaded, no `.aldo-memory` directory created. 16 minutes elapsed, no progress. MCP servers (aldo-fs, aldo-shell, aldo-git, aldo-memory) all spawned and connected to the worktree successfully, so MCP plumbing is fine. Likely culprits: local-discovery probe blocked on a non-Ollama source AbortController (the `parseDiscoverySources` defaults pass through every supported source even with `ALDO_LOCAL_DISCOVERY=ollama`?), or capability-class resolution selecting an unreachable model. Did NOT spend cycles tracking down — captured as a §13 follow-up: **the live:network harness needs an instrumentation/timeout layer + a fast-fail on per-stage progress.** Once that's in place a single smoke run will say "stuck in stage X for 60s" instead of going silent. The harness fixes above are the foundation that lets the next dogfood attempt actually produce a signal.

apps/api/src/runtime-bootstrap.ts:
- New exported `resetProviderStateCacheForLiveDryRun()` that nulls the module-level cache + in-flight promise. Production code never calls it.

apps/api/tests/agency-dry-run/healthz-db.ts:
- `DryRunResult.failureReason?: string` field added.
- `failure(...)` always sets `runStoreCount: 0` and a programmatic `failureReason`.
- `runLiveNetworkMode` calls `resetProviderStateCacheForLiveDryRun()` before resolving providerState.
- Imports updated.

apps/api/tests/agency-dry-run/healthz-db.test.ts:
- Env-gated smoke test now throws with `failureReason` + post-mortem prefix when the run fails before runtime, instead of crashing on undefined.

apps/api/tests/agency-dry-run/run-live-network.mjs (new):
- Operator-facing script that prints the live:network post-mortem + a tail line with `ok / runStoreCount / failureReason / spawn count`. Mirrors the existing `run-live.mjs` shape.

Verification:
- @aldo-ai/api: 542/542 tests pass + 1 properly skipped (was 542, structure unchanged for non-§12.5 cases).
- Typecheck clean.

Item #2 — §12.5 engagement-level budget cap, shipped:
- platform/storage/migrations/028_tenant_budget_caps.sql: new table `tenant_budget_caps (tenant_id, scope, usd_max, usd_window_start, hard_stop, created_at, updated_at)` with PK on (tenant_id, scope) and FK to tenants(id) ON DELETE CASCADE. v0 ships scope='engagement' only; column is in the schema so a future per-engagement-id row never needs a second migration.
- apps/api/src/tenant-budget-store.ts: `getTenantBudgetCap`, `upsertTenantBudgetCap`, `sumTenantSpendUsd`, `evaluateTenantBudget`, `assertWithinTenantBudget`, `TenantBudgetExceededError`. NULL cap = no check; soft cap (`hard_stop=false`) returns `allowed: true, softCap: true` so the existing `budget_threshold` notification pipe can fire without terminating the run. Window aggregation joins `usage_records.run_id → runs.tenant_id` (matches /v1/spend semantics).
- apps/api/src/routes/runs.ts: POST /v1/runs gate ahead of agent lookup. Returns HTTP 402 `tenant_budget_exceeded` with `capUsd` + `totalUsd` in details when over cap.
- apps/api/src/routes/tenants.ts: GET /v1/tenants/me/budget-cap (returns `{cap, currentUsd, softCap, allowed}`); PUT /v1/tenants/me/budget-cap (upsert with `usdMax | null`, `usdWindowStart`, `hardStop`).
- apps/api/tests/tenant-budget-cap.test.ts: 12 new tests covering store round-trip, idempotent upsert, clearing cap, soft cap (hardStop=false), window exclusion of pre-window spend, cross-tenant isolation, GET returns null by default, PUT upserts, POST /v1/runs returns 402 when cap reached.

Verification:
- @aldo-ai/api: 554/554 tests (was 542; +12 budget-cap tests; +0 in agency-dry-run by structural count). Typecheck clean.

Net of this turn: harness can now find what's wrong rather than crash on its own gaps; budget cap protects unsupervised runs from overnight runaway spend. Supervisor + iterative-run pre-step hooks deferred to a follow-up — the API-boundary check stops *new* runs but doesn't terminate in-flight ones. POST /v1/runs is the highest-leverage gate (every run starts there); follow-up adds the same check inside the iterative loop's pre-step termination predicate so a stuck run also stops.

Next: §14-A Hybrid CLI (apps/cli) — local-only agents run locally, cloud agents delegate to hosted ai.aldo.tech.
